================================================================================
FILE: src/hooks/useCountdown.js
================================================================================

1|import { useState, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
2|
3|function nextDeadline() {
4|  const now = new Date();
5|  const d = new Date(now);
6|  // Count down to the upcoming Sunday at 23:59 — aligns with the
7|  // banner label "Sale ends Sunday 23:59" so the countdown timer
8|  // always matches the stated deadline day.
9|  // If today IS Sunday, countdown to today 23:59 (not next Sunday).
10|  const daysUntilSunday = d.getDay() === 0 ? 0 : 7 - d.getDay();
11|  d.setDate(now.getDate() + daysUntilSunday);
12|  d.setHours(23, 59, 59, 999);
13|  return d;
14|}
15|
16|export function useCountdown() {
17|  const target = useRef(nextDeadline());
18|  const [left, setLeft] = useState(target.current - new Date());
19|
20|  useEffect(() => {
21|    const t = setInterval(() => {
22|      let ms = target.current - new Date();
23|      if (ms <= 0) { target.current = nextDeadline(); ms = target.current - new Date(); }
24|      setLeft(ms);
25|    }, 1000);
26|    return () => clearInterval(t);
27|  }, []);
28|
29|  const s = Math.max(0, Math.floor(left / 1000));
30|  return {
31|    d: Math.floor(s / 86400),
32|    h: Math.floor((s % 86400) / 3600),
33|    m: Math.floor((s % 3600) / 60),
34|    s: s % 60,
35|  };
36|}
37|
38|export const pad = (n) => String(n).padStart(2, '0');
39|
40|export const money = (n) => '€' + n.toFixed(2).replace(/\.00$/, '');
41|
42|export function discountPct(p) {
43|  return p.was ? Math.round((1 - p.price / p.was) * 100) : 0;
44|}
45|

30|/* ---------- Photo ---------- */
31|export function Photo({ id, hue, label, h = 320, img }) {
32|  const [loaded, setLoaded] = useState(false);
33|  const [errored, setErrored] = useState(false);
34|  const imgRef = useRef(null);
35|  const src = img || (IMG_BASE_URL ? `${IMG_BASE_URL}/${id}.webp` : null);
36|
37|  useEffect(() => {
38|    // Reset state when src changes (e.g. navigating between products)
39|    setLoaded(false);
40|    setErrored(false);
41|  }, [src]);
42|
43|  useEffect(() => {
44|    if (!imgRef.current || !src) return;
45|    const observer = new IntersectionObserver(
46|      ([entry]) => {
47|        if (entry.isIntersecting && imgRef.current) {
48|          imgRef.current.src = src;
49|          observer.disconnect();
50|        }
51|      },
52|      { rootMargin: '200px' }
53|    );
54|    observer.observe(imgRef.current);
55|    return () => observer.disconnect();
56|  }, [src]);
57|
58|  if (!src || errored) {
59|    // Colour-block placeholder (also used as error fallback when image load fails)
60|    const bg = `linear-gradient(150deg, oklch(0.72 0.17 ${hue}) 0%, oklch(0.55 0.2 ${(hue + 40) % 360}) 100%)`;
61|    return (
62|      <div className="rw-photo" style={{ height: h, position: 'relative' }}>
63|        <div className="rw-photo-bg" style={{ background: bg }}>
64|          <span className="rw-photo-word">{label}</span>
65|        </div>
66|      </div>
67|    );
68|  }
69|
70|  return (
71|    <div className="rw-photo" style={{ height: h, overflow: 'hidden', position: 'relative' }}>
72|      {!loaded && <div className="rw-skeleton" style={{ position: 'absolute', inset: 0 }} />}
73|      <img ref={imgRef} loading="lazy" className={`rw-img ${loaded ? 'loaded' : ''}`}
74|        alt={label}
75|        onLoad={() => setLoaded(true)}
76|        onError={() => { setErrored(true); setLoaded(true); }}
77|        style={{ position: 'absolute', inset: 0 }} />
78|    </div>
79|  );
80|}

111|export function Header({ cat, setCat, cartCount, onCart, wishlistCount, onWishlistOpen, query, setQuery, cats, version, onVersionClick, onReferral, isAdmin, searchSuggestions }) {
112|  const [focusedIdx, setFocusedIdx] = useState(-1);
113|  const suggestRef = useRef(null);
114|
115|  useEffect(() => {
116|    if (query) setFocusedIdx(-1);
117|  }, [query]);
118|
119|  useEffect(() => {
120|    const onClick = (e) => {
121|      if (suggestRef.current && !suggestRef.current.contains(e.target)) {
122|        setFocusedIdx(-1);
123|      }
124|    };
125|    document.addEventListener('mousedown', onClick);
126|    return () => document.removeEventListener('mousedown', onClick);
127|  }, []);
128|
129|  const hasSuggestions = query && searchSuggestions?.length > 0;
130|
131|  const handleKeyDown = (e) => {
132|    if (!hasSuggestions) {
133|      if (e.key === 'Escape' && query) { e.target.blur(); setQuery(''); }
134|      return;
135|    }
136|    if (e.key === 'ArrowDown') {
137|      e.preventDefault();
138|      setFocusedIdx(i => Math.min(i + 1, searchSuggestions.length - 1));
139|    } else if (e.key === 'ArrowUp') {
140|      e.preventDefault();
141|      setFocusedIdx(i => Math.max(i - 1, 0));
142|    } else if (e.key === 'Enter' && focusedIdx >= 0) {
143|      e.preventDefault();
144|      setQuery(searchSuggestions[focusedIdx].name);
145|      setFocusedIdx(-1);
146|    } else if (e.key === 'Escape') {
147|      setFocusedIdx(-1);
148|      e.target.blur();
149|      setQuery('');
150|    }
151|  };
152|
153|  return (
154|    <header className="rw-header">
155|      <div className="rw-header-row">
156|        <div className="rw-logo" style={{ cursor: 'pointer' }}
157|          onClick={() => { window.location.hash = ''; window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' }); window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('reset-store')); }}>REWIND<span>.</span></div>
158|        <nav className="rw-nav">
159|          {cats.map((c) => (

162|          ))}
163|        </nav>
164|        <div className="rw-header-actions">
165|          <div className="rw-search" ref={suggestRef} style={{position:'relative'}}>
166|            <Icon name="search" size={17} />
167|            <input value={query} onChange={(e) => setQuery(e.target.value)} onKeyDown={handleKeyDown} placeholder="Search" />
168|            {query && (
169|            <button onClick={() => setQuery('')}
170|              aria-label="Clear search"
171|              style={{
172|                background: 'none', border: 'none', cursor: 'pointer',
173|                padding: '2px', display: 'grid', placeItems: 'center',
174|                color: 'var(--muted)', opacity: 0.7,
175|                transition: 'opacity 0.15s',
176|              }}

178|              onMouseOut={e => e.target.style.opacity = '0.7'}>
179|                <Icon name="close" size={14} />
180|              </button>
181|            )}
182|            {hasSuggestions && (
183|              <div style={{

185|                background: 'var(--surface)', borderRadius: '10px', marginTop: '4px',
186|                boxShadow: '0 8px 24px rgba(0,0,0,.1)', overflow: 'hidden',
187|              }}>
188|                {searchSuggestions.map((s, i) => (
189|                  <button key={s.name} onClick={() => { setQuery(s.name); setFocusedIdx(-1); }}
190|                    onMouseOver={() => setFocusedIdx(i)}
191|                    style={{
192|                      display: 'block', width: '100%', padding: '8px 14px',
193|                      textAlign: 'left', border: 'none', cursor: 'pointer',
194|                      background: focusedIdx === i ? 'var(--line)' : 'transparent',

196|                      transition: 'background 0.1s',
197|                    }}>

200|                  </button>
201|                ))}
202|              </div>
203|            )}
204|          </div>

206|            <svg width={15} height={15} viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.7" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M17 21v-2a4 4 0 0 0-4-4H5a4 4 0 0 0-4 4v2"/><circle cx="9" cy="7" r="4"/><path d="M23 21v-2a4 4 0 0 0-3-3.87"/><path d="M16 3.13a4 4 0 0 1 0 7.75"/></svg>

223|/* ---------- TypingText (inline for no import breakage) ---------- */
224|export function TypingText({ texts, typingSpeed = 80, deleteSpeed = 40, pauseDuration = 2500 }) {
225|  const [text, setText] = useState('');
226|  const [ti, setTi] = useState(0);
227|  const [ci, setCi] = useState(0);
228|  const [deleting, setDeleting] = useState(false);
229|  useEffect(() => {
230|    if (!texts?.length) return;
231|    const current = texts[ti];
232|    const speed = deleting ? deleteSpeed : typingSpeed;
233|    const t = setTimeout(() => {
234|      if (!deleting) {
235|        if (ci < current.length) { setText(current.slice(0, ci + 1)); setCi(c => c + 1); }
236|        else setTimeout(() => setDeleting(true), pauseDuration);
237|      } else {
238|        if (ci > 0) { setText(current.slice(0, ci - 1)); setCi(c => c - 1); }
239|        else { setDeleting(false); setTi((ti + 1) % texts.length); }
240|      }
241|    }, speed);
242|    return () => clearTimeout(t);
243|  }, [ci, deleting, ti, texts, typingSpeed, deleteSpeed, pauseDuration]);
244|  return <span className="type-wrap">{text}<span className="type-cursor">|</span></span>;
245|}

8|/* ---------- LazyImage (for real product photos) ---------- */
9|function LazyImage({ src, alt, className }) {
10|  const [loaded, setLoaded] = useState(false);
11|  const [error, setError] = useState(false);
12|  const imgRef = useRef(null);
13|
14|  useEffect(() => {
15|    if (!imgRef.current) return;
16|    const observer = new IntersectionObserver(
17|      ([entry]) => {
18|        if (entry.isIntersecting && imgRef.current) {
19|          imgRef.current.src = src;
20|          observer.disconnect();
21|        }
22|      },
23|      { rootMargin: '200px' }
24|    );
25|    observer.observe(imgRef.current);
26|    return () => observer.disconnect();
27|  }, [src]);
28|
29|  return (
30|    <div className="rw-photo" style={{ position: 'relative', overflow: 'hidden' }}>
31|      {!loaded && !error && <div className="rw-skeleton" style={{ position: 'absolute', inset: 0 }} />}
32|      {error && (
33|        <div className="rw-photo-bg" style={{ background: 'var(--line)' }}>
34|          <span className="rw-photo-word" style={{ color: 'var(--muted)', mixBlendMode: 'normal' }}>{alt}</span>
35|        </div>
36|      )}
37|      <img ref={imgRef} className={`rw-img ${loaded ? 'loaded' : ''}`}
38|        alt={alt} onLoad={() => setLoaded(true)} onError={() => setError(true)}
39|        style={{ position: 'absolute', inset: 0 }} />
40|    </div>
41|  );

44|/* ---------- ProductCard ---------- */
45|export function ProductCard({ p, showCompare, showStock, onQuick, onAdd, wishlisted, onWishlist, onSelect, onCart }) {
46|  const low = p.stock > 0 && p.stock <= 5;
47|  const soldOut = p.stock === 0;
48|  const [added, setAdded] = useState(false);
49|  return (
50|    <article className="rw-card" style={{ opacity: soldOut ? 0.5 : 1 }}>
51|      <div className="rw-card-media" style={{ cursor: 'pointer' }} onClick={() => onSelect ? onSelect(p) : onQuick(p)}>
52|        <Photo id={p.id || p.product_id} hue={p.hue} label={p.name.toUpperCase()} h={340} img={p.img} />
53|        <div className="rw-card-tags">
54|          {showCompare && discountPct(p) > 0 && <span className="rw-tag rw-tag-sale">-{discountPct(p)}%</span>}
55|          {showStock && soldOut && <span className="rw-tag rw-tag-low">Sold out</span>}
56|          {showStock && low && !soldOut && <span className="rw-tag rw-tag-low">Only {p.stock} left</span>}
57|        </div>
58|        <button className="rw-card-quick" onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); onQuick(p); }}>Quick view</button>
59|        <button className={"rw-card-fav" + (wishlisted ? ' is-wishlisted' : '')}
60|          aria-label={wishlisted ? 'Remove from wishlist' : 'Save to wishlist'}
61|          style={{ color: wishlisted ? 'var(--accent)' : undefined }}
62|          onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); onWishlist(p); const btn = e.currentTarget; btn.classList.add('wiggle'); setTimeout(() => btn.classList.remove('wiggle'), 500); }}>
63|          <Icon name={wishlisted ? 'heartFilled' : 'heart'} size={17} />
64|        </button>
65|      </div>
66|      <div className="rw-card-body">
67|        <div className="rw-card-head">
68|          <h3 onClick={() => onSelect ? onSelect(p) : onQuick(p)} style={{ cursor: 'pointer' }}>{p.name}</h3>
69|          <span className="rw-card-cat">{p.cat}</span>
70|        </div>
71|        <div className="rw-card-foot">
72|          <div className="rw-price">
73|            <span className="rw-price-now">{money(p.price)}</span>
74|            {showCompare && p.was && <span className="rw-price-was">{money(p.was)}</span>}
75|          </div>
76|          {soldOut ? (
77|            <span className="rw-add" style={{ opacity: 0.35, cursor: 'default', background: 'none', display: 'grid', placeItems: 'center', width: '36px', height: '36px', borderRadius: '50%', border: '1.5px solid var(--line-2)' }}>
78|              <Icon name="close" size={16} />
79|            </span>
80|          ) : added ? (
81|            <button className="rw-add" style={{ background: 'var(--accent)', color: '#fff', border: 'none' }}
82|              onClick={onCart} aria-label="View in bag">
83|              <Icon name="bag" size={16} />
84|            </button>
85|          ) : (
86|          <button className="rw-add" onClick={() => { onAdd(p); setAdded(true); setTimeout(() => setAdded(false), 2000); }} aria-label={"Add " + p.name}>
87|            <Icon name="plus" size={18} />
88|          </button>
89|          )}
90|        </div>
91|        {soldOut ? (
92|          <div className="rw-card-ship" style={{color:'var(--muted)',fontSize:'12px',textAlign:'center',padding:'8px 0'}}>Unavailable</div>
93|        ) : (
94|        <div className="rw-card-ship">
95|          <Icon name="retrn" size={13} /> Free returns <span className="rw-price-was">€8</span>
96|        </div>
97|        )}
98|      </div>
99|    </article>
100|  );

103|/* ---------- ProductGrid ---------- */
104|export function ProductGrid({ products, wishlist, onWishlist, sort, query, onClearSearch, activeCat, activeBrand, onCart, cats, ...rest }) {
105|  if (products.length === 0) {
106|    const hasQuery = query && query.trim();
107|    const hasBrand = activeBrand;
108|    const hasCat = activeCat && activeCat !== 'All';
109|    let msg;
110|    if (hasQuery && hasBrand) {
111|      msg = `Nothing matched "${query.trim()}" for ${activeBrand}${hasCat ? ' in ' + activeCat : ''} — try a different term?`;
112|    } else if (hasQuery && hasCat) {
113|      msg = `Nothing matched "${query.trim()}" in ${activeCat} — try a different term?`;
114|    } else if (hasQuery) {
115|      msg = `Nothing matched "${query.trim()}" — try a different term?`;
116|    } else if (hasBrand) {
117|      msg = `No ${activeBrand} products${hasCat ? ' in ' + activeCat : ''} — try a different brand or category?`;
118|    } else if (hasCat) {
119|      msg = 'Nothing here in this category yet — try browsing all or checking back soon.';
120|    } else {
121|      msg = 'Nothing here yet — check back soon for new drops.';
122|    }
123|    const showClearFilters = hasQuery || hasBrand || hasCat;
124|    return (
125|      <div className="rw-empty">
126|        <span>{msg}</span>
127|        {showClearFilters && (
128|          <div style={{ marginTop: '14px' }}>
129|            <button className="rw-btn rw-btn-ghost" onClick={onClearSearch}
130|              style={{ fontSize: '13px', padding: '10px 18px' }}>
131|              ✕ Clear filters & show all
132|            </button>
133|          </div>
134|        )}
135|        {hasQuery && cats && cats.filter(c => c !== 'All').length > 0 && (
136|          <div style={{ marginTop: '20px' }}>
137|            <p style={{ fontSize: '12px', color: 'var(--muted)', marginBottom: '8px' }}>Browse categories:</p>
138|            <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '6px', flexWrap: 'wrap', justifyContent: 'center' }}>
139|              {cats.filter(c => c !== 'All').slice(0, 6).map(c => (
140|                <button key={c} onClick={() => { if (rest.onSetCat) rest.onSetCat(c); }}
141|                  style={{
142|                    padding: '6px 14px', borderRadius: '999px', border: '1px solid var(--line-2)',
143|                    background: 'var(--surface)', cursor: 'pointer', fontSize: '12px', fontWeight: 600,
144|                    color: 'var(--muted)', transition: 'all 0.15s',
145|                  }}
146|                  onMouseOver={e => { e.target.style.borderColor = 'var(--ink)'; e.target.style.color = 'var(--ink)'; }}
147|                  onMouseOut={e => { e.target.style.borderColor = 'var(--line-2)'; e.target.style.color = 'var(--muted)'; }}>
148|                  {c}
149|                </button>
150|              ))}
151|            </div>
152|          </div>
153|        )}
154|      </div>
155|    );
156|  }
157|  // Sort products
158|  let sorted = [...products];
159|  const isSorting = sort === 'price-asc' || sort === 'price-desc' || sort === 'name-asc' || sort === 'name-desc';
160|  if (sort === 'price-asc') sorted.sort((a, b) => a.price - b.price);
161|  else if (sort === 'price-desc') sorted.sort((a, b) => b.price - a.price);
162|  else if (sort === 'name-asc') sorted.sort((a, b) => (a.name || '').localeCompare(b.name || ''));
163|  else if (sort === 'name-desc') sorted.sort((a, b) => (b.name || '').localeCompare(a.name || ''));
164|
165|  // When sorting is active, render a single flat grid so the sort order is respected globally.
166|  if (isSorting) {
167|    return (
168|      <div>
169|        <div className="rw-grid">
170|          {sorted.map((p) => (
171|            <ProductCard key={p.id || p.product_id} p={p} wishlisted={wishlist?.includes(p.id || p.product_id)} onWishlist={onWishlist}
172|              showCompare={rest.showCompare} showStock={rest.showStock} onQuick={rest.onQuick} onAdd={rest.onAdd} onSelect={rest.onSelect} onCart={onCart} />
173|          ))}
174|        </div>
175|      </div>
176|    );
177|  }
178|
179|  // Group products by category, then flatten with headers (Featured view)
180|  const grouped = {};
181|  sorted.forEach(p => {
182|    const cat = p.cat || 'Other';
183|    if (!grouped[cat]) grouped[cat] = [];
184|    grouped[cat].push(p);
185|  });
186|
187|  const sections = Object.entries(grouped).map(([cat, items]) => {
188|    // When browsing a specific category (not "All"), the category is already
189|    // shown in the page title — omit it from section headers to reduce noise.
190|    const isCurrentCat = activeCat && activeCat !== 'All' && cat === activeCat;
191|    const label = isCurrentCat ? '' : cat;
192|    return { label, items };
193|  });
194|
195|  return (
196|    <div className="rw-grid">
197|      {sections.map((s, i) => (
198|        <React.Fragment key={i}>
199|          {s.label && (
200|            <h3 className="rw-section-head">
201|              {s.label}
202|            </h3>
203|          )}
204|          {s.items.map((p) => (
205|            <ProductCard key={p.id || p.product_id} p={p} wishlisted={wishlist?.includes(p.id || p.product_id)} onWishlist={onWishlist}
206|              showCompare={rest.showCompare} showStock={rest.showStock} onQuick={rest.onQuick} onAdd={rest.onAdd} onSelect={rest.onSelect} onCart={onCart} />
207|          ))}
208|        </React.Fragment>
209|      ))}
210|    </div>
211|  );
212|}

214|/* ---------- QuickView ---------- */
215|export function QuickView({ p, showCompare, showStock, onClose, onAdd }) {
216|  const [size, setSize] = useState(null);
217|  const [showQvMenu, setShowQvMenu] = useState(false);
218|  // Reset size selection when the product changes — prevents stale size
219|  // from a previous product (e.g. shoe size "42" persisting after switching
220|  // to a jersey with S/M/L/XL sizes).
221|  useEffect(() => { setSize(null); }, [p?.id || p?.product_id]);
222|  if (!p) return null;
223|  const low = p.stock > 0 && p.stock <= 5;
224|  const soldOut = p.stock === 0;
225|  return (
226|    <div className="rw-modal-wrap" onClick={onClose}>

252|              }
253|            }}
254|              onMouseOver={e => e.target.style.background = 'var(--line)'}
255|              onMouseOut={e => e.target.style.background = 'transparent'}
256|              style={{ display: 'block', width: '100%', padding: '8px 14px', textAlign: 'left', border: 'none', background: 'transparent', cursor: 'pointer', fontSize: '13px', fontWeight: 600, transition: 'background 0.1s' }}>
257|              🗑 Delete
258|            </button>

260|              localStorage.setItem('rw_edit_product', p.id || p.product_id);
261|              window.location.hash = '#admin';

263|              onMouseOver={e => e.target.style.background = 'var(--line)'}

306|/* ---------- CartDrawer ---------- */
307|export function CartDrawer({ open, items, onClose, onQty, onRemove, onCheckout, showToast, pendingRemove, onCancelRemove }) {
308|  const subtotal = items.reduce((s, it) => s + it.price * it.qty, 0);
309|  const FREE_THRESHOLD = 150;
310|  const freeProgress = Math.min(100, (subtotal / FREE_THRESHOLD) * 100);
311|  const freeLeft = Math.max(0, FREE_THRESHOLD - subtotal);
312|
313|  return (
314|    <>
315|      <div className={"rw-scrim" + (open ? " is-on" : "")} onClick={onClose} />
316|      <div className={"rw-drawer" + (open ? " is-on" : "")}>
317|        <div className="rw-drawer-head">
318|          <h3>Bag</h3>
319|          <button onClick={onClose} aria-label="Close"><Icon name="close" size={20} /></button>
320|        </div>
321|        {items.length > 0 && subtotal < FREE_THRESHOLD ? (
322|          <div className="rw-freebar">
323|            <Icon name="truck" size={14} /> Add <b>{money(freeLeft)}</b> more for free shipping
324|            <div className="rw-freebar-track"><div style={{ width: freeProgress + '%' }} /></div>
325|          </div>
326|        ) : subtotal >= FREE_THRESHOLD && items.length > 0 && (
327|          <div className="rw-freebar" style={{ color: 'var(--ink)' }}>
328|            <Icon name="check" size={14} /> <b>Free shipping unlocked!</b> 🎉
329|          </div>
330|        )}
331|        {items.length === 0 ? (
332|          <div className="rw-drawer-empty">
333|            <Icon name="bag" size={36} />
334|            <p>Your bag is empty</p>
335|          </div>
336|        ) : (
337|          <div className="rw-drawer-items">
338|            {items.map((it) => (
339|              <div key={it.key} className="rw-line">
340|                <div className="rw-line-media">
341|                  <Photo id={it.id + "-cart"} hue={it.hue} label="" h={74} img={it.img} />
342|                </div>
343|                <div className="rw-line-info">
344|                  <div className="rw-line-top">
345|                    <h4>{it.name}</h4>
346|                    <button className="rw-line-x" onClick={() => onRemove(it.key, it.name)} aria-label="Remove">
347|                      <Icon name="close" size={15} />
348|                    </button>
349|                  </div>
350|                  <div className="rw-line-meta">{it.size}</div>
351|                  <div className="rw-line-bot">
352|                    <div className="rw-qty">
353|                      <button onClick={() => onQty(it.key, -1)} aria-label="Decrease"><Icon name="minus" size={13} /></button>
354|                      <span>{it.qty}</span>
355|                      <button onClick={() => onQty(it.key, 1)} aria-label="Increase"><Icon name="plus" size={13} /></button>
356|                    </div>
357|                    <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '6px' }}>
358|                      {it.was && (
359|                        <span style={{ fontSize: '12px', color: 'var(--muted)', textDecoration: 'line-through' }}>
360|                          {money(it.was * it.qty)}
361|                        </span>
362|                      )}
363|                      <span className="rw-line-price">{money(it.price * it.qty)}</span>
364|                    </div>
365|                  </div>
366|                </div>
367|              </div>
368|            ))}
369|          </div>
370|        )}
371|        {items.length > 0 && (
372|          <div className="rw-drawer-foot">
373|            <div className="rw-subtotal">
374|              <span>Subtotal</span>
375|              <b>{money(subtotal)}</b>
376|            </div>
377|            <button className="rw-btn rw-btn-pri rw-btn-full" onClick={onCheckout}>
378|              Checkout <Icon name="arrow" size={16} />
379|            </button>
380|            <div className="rw-paystrip">
381|              {REWIND_PAYMENTS.map((pm) => (
382|                <span key={pm.id} className="rw-paychip">{pm.label}</span>
383|              ))}
384|            </div>
385|          </div>
386|        )}
387|      </div>
388|      {pendingRemove && (
389|        <div className="rw-scrim is-on" onClick={onCancelRemove} />
390|      )}
391|      {pendingRemove && (
392|        <div style={{ position: 'fixed', top: '50%', left: '50%', transform: 'translate(-50%,-50%)', zIndex: 52, background: 'var(--bg)', borderRadius: '12px', padding: '24px', maxWidth: '340px', width: '90vw', boxShadow: '0 20px 60px rgba(0,0,0,0.25)', textAlign: 'center' }}>
393|          <p style={{ fontSize: '14px', fontWeight: 600, margin: '0 0 16px', color: 'var(--ink)' }}>Remove "{pendingRemove.name}" from your bag?</p>
394|          <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '10px', justifyContent: 'center' }}>
395|            <button onClick={() => { onRemove(pendingRemove.key, pendingRemove.name); onCancelRemove(); }} style={{ padding: '10px 24px', borderRadius: '10px', border: 'none', background: 'var(--accent, #FF4D14)', color: '#fff', fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '14px', cursor: 'pointer' }}>Remove</button>
396|            <button onClick={onCancelRemove} style={{ padding: '10px 24px', borderRadius: '10px', border: '1px solid var(--line)', background: 'var(--surface)', color: 'var(--muted)', fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '14px', cursor: 'pointer' }}>Cancel</button>
397|          </div>
398|        </div>
399|      )}
400|    </>
401|  );

404|/* ---------- Checkout ---------- */
405|export function Checkout({ open, items, onClose, onPlaced, userEmail, showToast, orderNumber: orderNumberProp, onInfo }) {
406|  const [payment, setPayment] = useState('card');
407|  const [placed, setPlaced] = useState(false);
408|  const [processing, setProcessing] = useState(false);
409|  const [cardValid, setCardValid] = useState(false);
410|  const [promoData, setPromoData] = useState(null);
411|  const [promoValidating, setPromoValidating] = useState(false);
412|  const [promo, setPromo] = useState('');
413|  const [payError, setPayError] = useState('');
414|  const [orderNum, setOrderNum] = useState('');
415|  // Referral state
416|  const [referralCode, setReferralCode] = useState('');
417|  const [appliedReferral, setAppliedReferral] = useState(null);
418|  const [referralLoading, setReferralLoading] = useState(false);
419|  const [referralError, setReferralError] = useState('');
420|  const paymentRef = useRef(null);
421|  const [saveInfo, setSaveInfo] = useState(false);
422|  const [formFields, setFormFields] = useState({ email: '', name: '', address: '', postal: '', city: '', country: '' });
423|
424|  // Generate order number when checkout opens
425|  useEffect(() => {
426|    if (open) {
427|      setOrderNum('RW-' + String(Date.now()).slice(-8));
428|    }
429|  }, [open]);
430|  const setField = (key) => (e) => setFormFields((prev) => ({ ...prev, [key]: e.target.value }));
431|
432|  if (!open) return null;
433|  if (placed) {
434|    return (
435|      <div className="rw-checkout" style={{ position: 'relative', overflow: 'hidden' }}>
436|        {Array.from({ length: 40 }).map((_, i) => (
437|          <div key={i} style={{
438|            position: 'absolute', top: '-10px', left: (Math.random() * 100) + '%',
439|            width: (Math.random() * 8 + 4) + 'px', height: (Math.random() * 8 + 4) + 'px',
440|            borderRadius: '2px',
441|            background: ['#FF4D14','#D4AF37','#FF6B35','#FFB800','#FF4081','#00C853'][i % 6],
442|            animation: 'confettiFall ' + (Math.random() * 2 + 2) + 's ease-in ' + (Math.random() * 0.5) + 's infinite',
443|            zIndex: 0, pointerEvents: 'none',
444|          }} />
445|        ))}
446|        <div className="rw-checkout-bar" style={{ position: 'relative', zIndex: 1 }}>
447|          <div className="rw-logo" style={{ cursor: 'pointer' }}
448|            onClick={() => { window.location.hash = ''; window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('reset-store')); onPlaced(); }}>REWIND<span>.</span></div>
449|          <button className="rw-btn rw-btn-ghost" onClick={onPlaced}>Close</button>
450|        </div>
451|        <div className="rw-confirm">
452|          <div className="rw-confirm-mark"><Icon name="check" size={36} /></div>
453|          <h2>Order confirmed</h2>
454|          <p>Thanks for your order! We'll send you a shipping confirmation once your items are on their way.</p>
455|          <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '8px', justifyContent: 'center', marginTop: '4px' }}>
456|            <div className="rw-confirm-num">{orderNum}</div>
457|            <button onClick={(e) => { const btn = e.currentTarget; navigator.clipboard.writeText(orderNum).then(() => { btn.textContent = '✓'; setTimeout(() => { btn.textContent = '⎘'; }, 1200); }).catch(() => { btn.textContent = '✗'; setTimeout(() => { btn.textContent = '⎘'; }, 1200); }); }}
458|              style={{ width: '28px', height: '28px', borderRadius: '8px', border: '1px solid var(--line-2)', background: 'var(--surface)', cursor: 'pointer', fontSize: '13px', display: 'grid', placeItems: 'center', color: 'var(--muted)', transition: 'background 0.15s' }}
459|              onMouseOver={e => e.target.style.background = 'var(--line)'}
460|              onMouseOut={e => e.target.style.background = 'var(--surface)'}>
461|              ⎘
462|            </button>
463|          </div>
464|          <p style={{ fontSize: '12px', color: 'var(--muted)', marginTop: '12px' }}>A confirmation has been sent to your email</p>
465|          <button className="rw-btn rw-btn-pri" onClick={onPlaced}>Continue shopping</button>
466|        </div>
467|      </div>
468|    );
469|  }
470|
471|  const subtotal = items.reduce((s, it) => s + it.price * it.qty, 0);
472|  const shipping = subtotal >= 150 ? 0 : 8;
473|  let discountPrice = subtotal;
474|  let discountShipping = shipping;
475|  let discountLabel = null;
476|  if (promoData?.valid) {
477|    if (promoData.type === 'percent') {
478|      discountPrice = Math.round(subtotal * (100 - promoData.value)) / 100;
479|      discountLabel = `${promoData.value}% off`;
480|    } else if (promoData.type === 'free_shipping') {
481|      discountShipping = 0;
482|      discountLabel = 'Free shipping';
483|    }
484|  }
485|  // Apply referral discount on top of promo (if any)
486|  let referralDiscountLabel = null;
487|  let referralDiscountAmount = 0;
488|  if (appliedReferral?.discount) {
489|    referralDiscountAmount = Math.round(discountPrice * (appliedReferral.discount / 100) * 100) / 100;
490|    discountPrice = Math.round((discountPrice - referralDiscountAmount) * 100) / 100;
491|    referralDiscountLabel = `${appliedReferral.discount}% off (referral)`;
492|  }
493|  const finalTotal = discountPrice + discountShipping;
494|
495|  // Referral code handler
496|  async function handleReferralApply(code) {
497|    if (!code) {
498|      // Remove referral
499|      setAppliedReferral(null);
500|      setReferralCode('');
501|      setReferralError('');
502|      return;
503|    }
504|    if (!formFields.email?.trim()) {
505|      setReferralError('Please enter your email first');
506|      return;
507|    }
508|    setReferralLoading(true);
509|    setReferralError('');
510|    try {
511|      const r = await fetch('/api/referral/validate', {
512|        method: 'POST',
513|        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
514|        body: JSON.stringify({ code, email: formFields.email.trim() }),
515|      });
516|      const d = await r.json();
517|      if (d.valid) {
518|        setAppliedReferral({ code: code.toUpperCase(), discount: d.discount });
519|        setReferralCode(code);
520|        setReferralError('');
521|      } else {
522|        setAppliedReferral(null);
523|        setReferralError(d.error || 'Invalid referral code');
524|      }
525|    } catch {
526|      setReferralError('Network error — try again');
527|      setAppliedReferral(null);
528|    }
529|    setReferralLoading(false);
530|  }
531|
532|  async function handlePay() {
533|    setProcessing(true);
534|    setPayError('');
535|    // Client-side field validation before hitting the API
536|    const missing = [];
537|    if (!formFields.email?.trim()) missing.push('Email');
538|    else if (!/^\S+@\S+\.\S+$/.test(formFields.email.trim())) {
539|      setPayError('Please enter a valid email address');
540|      setProcessing(false);
541|      return;
542|    }
543|    if (!formFields.name?.trim()) missing.push('Full name');
544|    if (!formFields.address?.trim()) missing.push('Address');
545|    if (!formFields.postal?.trim()) missing.push('Postal code');
546|    if (!formFields.city?.trim()) missing.push('City');
547|    if (!formFields.country?.trim()) missing.push('Country');
548|    if (missing.length > 0) {
549|      setPayError('Please fill in: ' + missing.join(', '));
550|      setProcessing(false);
551|      return;
552|    }
553|    const email = formFields.email;
554|    // Check if email is blocked BEFORE persisting any data to localStorage —
555|    // prevents blocked users' personal info from being saved locally.
556|    try {
557|      const br = await fetch('/api/check-blocked-email', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ email }) });
558|      const bd = await br.json();
559|      if (bd.blocked) {
560|        setProcessing(false);
561|        if (showToast) {
562|          showToast('🚫 Your email has been blocked. Contact orders@rewind-stores.com to appeal.', null, 8000);
563|        } else {
564|          alert('🚫 Your email has been blocked.\nPlease contact orders@rewind-stores.com to appeal.');
565|        }
566|        return;
567|      }
568|    } catch {}
569|    // Save delivery info to localStorage if checkbox is checked
570|    if (saveInfo) {
571|      localStorage.setItem('rw_checkout_save_info', 'true');
572|      const { email, name, address, postal, city, country } = formFields;
573|      if (email || name || address || postal || city || country) {
574|        localStorage.setItem('rw_checkout_info', JSON.stringify({ email, name, address, postal, city, country }));
575|      }
576|    } else {
577|      localStorage.setItem('rw_checkout_save_info', 'false');
578|      localStorage.removeItem('rw_checkout_info');
579|    }
580|    // Use the orderNum already set in state (generated when checkout opened)
581|    const currentOrderNum = orderNum;
582|    try {
583|      // Process payment via Stripe Elements inline
584|      const payResult = await paymentRef.current?.pay({
585|        name: formFields.name,
586|        email: formFields.email,
587|        address: formFields.address,
588|        city: formFields.city,
589|        postal: formFields.postal,
590|        country: formFields.country,
591|      });
592|
593|      if (!payResult || payResult.error) {
594|        setPayError(payResult?.error || 'Payment failed — please try again');
595|        setProcessing(false);
596|        return;
597|      }
598|
599|      if (payResult.success) {
600|        // Payment succeeded — save order to Supabase and send confirmation
601|        setOrderNum(currentOrderNum);
602|        setCardValid(false);
603|
604|        // Order save + confirmation email are handled server-side by the
605|        // Stripe webhook (payment_intent.succeeded) once payment is verified —
606|        // never trust the client's own "success" signal for fulfillment.
607|
608|        // Record referral redemption (if a referral code was applied)
609|        if (referralCode) {
610|          fetch('/api/referral/apply', {
611|            method: 'POST',
612|            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
613|            body: JSON.stringify({
614|              code: referralCode,
615|              refereeEmail: formFields.email,
616|              orderNum: currentOrderNum,
617|              refereeName: formFields.name,
618|              refereeAddress: [formFields.address, formFields.postal, formFields.city, formFields.country].filter(Boolean).join(', '),
619|            }),
620|          }).catch(e => console.warn('Referral apply failed:', e));
621|        }
622|
623|        // Show confirmation
624|        setProcessing(false);
625|        setPlaced(true);
626|      } else {
627|        setPayError('Payment could not be completed. Please try again.');
628|        setProcessing(false);
629|      }
630|    } catch (e) {
631|      setProcessing(false);
632|      setPayError('Payment could not be processed — please check your details and try again.');
633|      console.warn('Payment error:', e);
634|    }
635|  }
636|
637|  return (
638|    <div className="rw-checkout">
639|      <div className="rw-checkout-bar">
640|        <div className="rw-logo" style={{ cursor: 'pointer' }}
641|          onClick={() => { window.location.hash = ''; window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('reset-store')); onClose(); }}>REWIND<span>.</span></div>
642|        <button className="rw-btn rw-btn-ghost" onClick={onClose}>Back</button>
643|      </div>
644|      <div className="rw-checkout-grid">
645|        <div className="rw-checkout-main">
646|          <div className="rw-co-sec">
647|            <h3>Contact</h3>
648|            <input className="rw-input" type="email" placeholder="Email" value={formFields.email} onChange={setField('email')} autoComplete="email" />
649|          </div>
650|          <div className="rw-co-sec">
651|            <h3>Promo code</h3>
652|            <div style={{ position: 'relative' }}>
653|              <input className="rw-input" placeholder="Enter code" value={promo} onChange={e => setPromo(e.target.value)}
654|                style={{ paddingRight: promo ? '32px' : undefined }} />
655|              {promo && (
656|                <button onClick={() => setPromo('')}
657|                  aria-label="Clear promo code"
658|                  style={{
659|                    position: 'absolute', right: '8px', top: '50%', transform: 'translateY(-50%)',
660|                    background: 'none', border: 'none', cursor: 'pointer',
661|                    padding: '4px', display: 'grid', placeItems: 'center',
662|                    color: 'var(--muted)', opacity: 0.7,
663|                    transition: 'opacity 0.15s',
664|                  }}
665|                  onMouseOver={e => e.target.style.opacity = '1'}
666|                  onMouseOut={e => e.target.style.opacity = '0.7'}>
667|                  <Icon name="close" size={14} />
668|                </button>
669|              )}
670|            </div>
671|            {promoValidating && (
672|              <span style={{color: 'var(--muted)', fontSize: '13px', marginTop: '6px', display: 'block', fontWeight: 500}}>
673|                ⏳ Validating...
674|              </span>
675|            )}
676|            {promoData?.valid && (
677|              <span style={{color: 'var(--ink)', fontSize: '13px', marginTop: '6px', display: 'block', fontWeight: 600}}>
678|                ✓ {promoData.type === 'percent' ? `${promoData.value}% off applied!` : 'Free shipping applied!'}
679|              </span>
680|            )}
681|            {promoData && !promoData.valid && promo.trim() && !promoValidating && (
682|              <span style={{color: 'var(--accent)', fontSize: '13px', marginTop: '6px', display: 'block'}}>
683|                Invalid promo code
684|              </span>
685|            )}
686|          </div>
687|          <ReferralInput
688|            onApply={handleReferralApply}
689|            appliedReferral={appliedReferral}
690|            referralDiscount={appliedReferral?.discount || 0}
691|            referralLoading={referralLoading}
692|            referralError={referralError} />
693|          <div className="rw-co-sec">
694|            <h3>Delivery</h3>
695|            <input className="rw-input" type="text" placeholder="Full name" value={formFields.name} onChange={setField('name')} autoComplete="name" />
696|            <input className="rw-input" type="text" placeholder="Address" value={formFields.address} onChange={setField('address')} autoComplete="street-address" />
697|            <div className="rw-input-row">
698|              <input className="rw-input" type="text" placeholder="Postal code" value={formFields.postal} onChange={setField('postal')} autoComplete="postal-code" />
699|              <input className="rw-input" type="text" placeholder="City" value={formFields.city} onChange={setField('city')} autoComplete="address-level2" />
700|            </div>
701|            <input className="rw-input" type="text" placeholder="Country" value={formFields.country} onChange={setField('country')} autoComplete="country-name" />
702|          </div>
703|        </div>
704|        <div className="rw-checkout-summary">
705|          <h3>Order summary</h3>
706|          <div className="rw-sum-items">
707|            {items.map((it) => (
708|              <div key={it.key} className="rw-sum-line">
709|                <div className="rw-sum-media">
710|                  <Photo id={it.id + "-sum"} hue={it.hue} label="" h={52} img={it.img} />
711|                  {it.qty > 1 && <span className="rw-sum-qty">{it.qty}</span>}
712|                </div>
713|                <div className="rw-sum-info">
714|                  <h4>{it.name}</h4>
715|                  <span>{it.size}</span>
716|                </div>
717|                <span className="rw-sum-price">{money(it.price * it.qty)}</span>
718|              </div>
719|            ))}
720|          </div>
721|          <div className="rw-sum-rows">
722|            <div><span>Subtotal</span><span>{money(subtotal)}</span></div>
723|            {promoData?.valid && promoData.type === 'percent' && (
724|              <div style={{color: 'var(--ink)', fontSize: '13px', fontWeight: 600}}>
725|                <span>{discountLabel}</span><span>-{money(subtotal - discountPrice)}</span>
726|              </div>
727|            )}
728|            {referralDiscountLabel && (
729|              <div style={{color: '#0E9F6E', fontSize: '13px', fontWeight: 600}}>
730|                <span>{referralDiscountLabel}</span><span>-{money(referralDiscountAmount)}</span>
731|              </div>
732|            )}
733|            <div><span>Shipping</span><span>{discountShipping === 0 ? (promoData?.valid && promoData.type === 'free_shipping' ? 'Free 🎉' : 'Free') : money(discountShipping)}</span></div>
734|          </div>
735|          <div className="rw-sum-total">
736|            <div><span>Total</span><b>{money(finalTotal)}</b></div>
737|          </div>
738|          <button className="rw-btn rw-btn-pri rw-btn-full"
739|            disabled={processing || (payment === 'card' && !cardValid)}
740|            onClick={handlePay}>
741|            {processing ? <><i className="rw-spinner" /> Processing…</> : `Pay ${money(finalTotal)}`}
742|          </button>
743|          <div className="rw-co-trust">
744|            <Icon name="check" size={13} /> Secured with 256-bit SSL
745|          </div>
746|        </div>
747|      </div>
748|      <div className="rw-checkout-payment">
749|        <h3 style={{ fontSize: '19px', fontWeight: 700, marginBottom: '14px' }}>Payment</h3>
750|        <div className="rw-pay-grid">
751|          {REWIND_PAYMENTS.map((pm) => (
752|            <button key={pm.id} className={"rw-pay" + (payment === pm.id ? " is-on" : "")}
753|              onClick={() => setPayment(pm.id)}>
754|              <div className="rw-pay-radio">{payment === pm.id && <Icon name="check" size={13} />}</div>
755|              <div className="rw-pay-label">
756|                {pm.label}
757|                <small>{pm.sub}</small>
758|              </div>
759|            </button>
760|          ))}
761|        </div>
762|        {payment === 'card' && (
763|          <div className="rw-card-fields">
764|            <PaymentCard
765|              ref={paymentRef}
766|              amount={money(finalTotal)}
767|              stripeKey={import.meta.env.VITE_STRIPE_PUBLISHABLE_KEY}
768|              orderNum={orderNum}
769|              email={formFields.email}
770|              name={formFields.name}
771|              address={[formFields.address, formFields.postal, formFields.city, formFields.country].filter(Boolean).join(', ')}
772|              items={items}
773|              promoCode={promo}
774|              onChange={({ valid }) => setCardValid(valid)}
775|            />
776|          </div>
777|        )}
778|        <div className="rw-co-config">
779|          {payment === 'payconiq' && 'Scan the QR code with Payconiq to complete payment.'}
780|          {payment === 'applepay' && 'Complete payment with Face ID or Touch ID.'}
781|          {payment === 'klarna' && 'Pay in 3 interest-free instalments.'}
782|          {payment === 'bancontact' && 'You will be redirected to your bank to confirm.'}
783|          {payment === 'paypal' && 'You will be redirected to PayPal to complete your purchase.'}
784|        </div>
785|        <label className="rw-check">
786|          <input type="checkbox" checked={saveInfo} onChange={(e) => setSaveInfo(e.target.checked)} /> Save my info for next time
787|        </label>
788|        <p style={{ fontSize: '11.5px', color: 'var(--muted)', marginTop: '12px', lineHeight: '1.5' }}>
789|          By proceeding, you agree to our <button type="button" onClick={() => onInfo && onInfo('privacy')}
790|          style={{ textDecoration: 'underline', cursor: 'pointer', background: 'none', border: 'none', color: 'var(--muted)', fontWeight: 600, padding: 0, fontSize: 'inherit' }}>Privacy Policy</button>.
791|        </p>
792|      </div>
793|    </div>

858|export function SignupModal({ open, onClose, onSignup }) {
859|  const [email, setEmail] = useState('');
860|  const [agreePolicy, setAgreePolicy] = useState(false);
861|  const [acceptMarketing, setAcceptMarketing] = useState(false);
862|  const [error, setError] = useState('');
863|  const [showPolicy, setShowPolicy] = useState(false);
864|
865|  // Reset form fields whenever the modal opens — prevents stale data from a
866|  // previous session persisting when the user reopens the signup modal.
867|  useEffect(() => {
868|    if (open) {
869|      setEmail('');
870|      setAgreePolicy(false);
871|      setAcceptMarketing(false);
872|      setError('');
873|      setShowPolicy(false);
874|    }
875|  }, [open]);
876|
877|  if (!open) return null;
878|
879|  function handleSubmit(e) {
880|    e.preventDefault();
881|    setError('');
882|    if (!email.trim() || !/\S+@\S+\.\S+/.test(email)) {
883|      setError('Please enter a valid email address');
884|      return;
885|    }
886|    if (!agreePolicy) {
887|      setError('Please agree to the privacy policy');
888|      return;
889|    }
890|    onSignup({ email: email.trim(), acceptMarketing });
891|  }
892|
893|  return (
894|    <div className="rw-modal-wrap" onClick={onClose}>
895|      <div className="rw-modal rw-modal--signup" onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
896|        style={{ maxWidth: '460px', gridTemplateColumns: '1fr' }}>
897|        <button className="rw-modal-x" onClick={onClose} aria-label="Close"><Icon name="close" size={18} /></button>
898|        {showPolicy ? (
899|          <div className="rw-modal-info">
900|            <h2 style={{ fontSize: '24px', marginBottom: '16px' }}>Privacy Policy</h2>
901|            <div style={{ fontFamily: 'var(--font-body)', color: 'var(--muted)', fontSize: '14px', lineHeight: '1.7', whiteSpace: 'pre-wrap' }}>
902|              {POLICY_TEXT}
903|            </div>
904|            <button className="rw-btn rw-btn-pri rw-btn-full" style={{ marginTop: '20px' }}
905|              onClick={() => setShowPolicy(false)}>Back</button>
906|          </div>
907|        ) : (
908|          <div className="rw-modal-info">
909|            <h2 style={{ fontSize: '24px', marginBottom: '6px' }}>Save to wishlist</h2>
910|            <p style={{ color: 'var(--muted)', fontSize: '14px', marginBottom: '20px' }}>
911|              Sign up with your email to save items and come back later.
912|            </p>
913|            <form onSubmit={handleSubmit}>
914|              <input className="rw-input" type="email" placeholder="Your email"
915|                value={email} onChange={(e) => setEmail(e.target.value)}
916|                style={{ marginBottom: '14px' }} autoFocus />
917|              <label className="rw-check" style={{ marginBottom: '10px' }}>
918|                <input type="checkbox" checked={agreePolicy}
919|                  onChange={(e) => setAgreePolicy(e.target.checked)} />
920|                <span>I agree to the <button type="button" onClick={() => setShowPolicy(true)}
921|                  style={{ textDecoration: 'underline', cursor: 'pointer', background: 'none', border: 'none', color: 'var(--ink)', fontWeight: 600, padding: 0, fontSize: 'inherit' }}>
922|                  privacy policy</button></span>
923|              </label>
924|              <label className="rw-check" style={{ marginBottom: '16px' }}>
925|                <input type="checkbox" checked={acceptMarketing}
926|                  onChange={(e) => setAcceptMarketing(e.target.checked)} />
927|                <span>Email me about new drops & exclusive offers</span>
928|              </label>
929|              {error && <p style={{ color: 'var(--accent)', fontSize: '13px', marginBottom: '10px' }}>{error}</p>}
930|              <button type="submit" className="rw-btn rw-btn-pri rw-btn-full">
931|                Sign up & save <Icon name="heart" size={15} />
932|              </button>
933|            </form>
934|          </div>
935|        )}
936|      </div>
937|    </div>
938|  );

941|/* ---------- Wishlist Drawer ---------- */
942|export function WishlistDrawer({ open, items, customProducts, onClose, onRemove, onAddToCart, onSelect, onCartOpen, showToast }) {
943|  const allProducts = useMemo(() => [...REWIND_PRODUCTS, ...(customProducts || [])], [customProducts]);
944|  const wishlistItems = items.map((id) => allProducts.find((p) => p.id === id || p.product_id === id)).filter(Boolean);
945|  const [selected, setSelected] = useState([]);
946|  // Track which wishlist item has its inline size picker open (stored as product id)
947|  const [choosingSize, setChoosingSize] = useState(null);
948|  // Reset size picker when drawer opens — prevents a stale open picker from a
949|  // previous session (where the user opened a size picker then closed the drawer
950|  // without selecting a size) from persisting when the drawer is reopened.
951|  useEffect(() => {
952|    if (open) setChoosingSize(null);
953|  }, [open]);
954|
955|  // Custom products (from Supabase) use product_id as their key, not id.
956|  // Always use getId(p) to get the canonical wishlist identifier.
957|  const getId = (p) => p.id || p.product_id;
958|
959|  const toggleSelect = (id) => {
960|    setSelected(prev => prev.includes(id) ? prev.filter(x => x !== id) : [...prev, id]);
961|  };
962|  const addSelectedToCart = () => {
963|    const toAdd = wishlistItems.filter(p => selected.includes(getId(p)));
964|    if (toAdd.length === 0) return;
965|    // Single item: open inline size picker instead of silently defaulting size
966|    if (toAdd.length === 1) {
967|      setChoosingSize(getId(toAdd[0]));
968|      setSelected([]);
969|      return;
970|    }
971|    // Multiple items: add all with default sizes but warn explicitly
972|    if (onAddToCart) {
973|      toAdd.forEach(p => onAddToCart(p));
974|      setSelected([]);
975|      if (onCartOpen) onCartOpen();
976|      if (showToast) {
977|        setTimeout(() => showToast(toAdd.length + ' items added — each used the first available size'), 50);
978|      }
979|    }
980|  };
981|
982|  return (
983|    <>
984|      <div className={"rw-scrim" + (open ? " is-on" : "")} onClick={onClose} />
985|      <div className={"rw-drawer" + (open ? " is-on" : "")} style={{ width: '400px' }}>
986|        <div className="rw-drawer-head">
987|          <h3>Wishlist <span>({wishlistItems.length})</span></h3>
988|          <button onClick={onClose} aria-label="Close"><Icon name="close" size={20} /></button>
989|        </div>
990|        {wishlistItems.length > 0 && (
991|          <div style={{ padding: '8px 16px', borderBottom: '1px solid var(--line)', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '8px' }}>
992|            <input type="checkbox" checked={selected.length === wishlistItems.length && wishlistItems.length > 0}
993|              onChange={() => { if (selected.length === wishlistItems.length) { setSelected([]); } else { setSelected(wishlistItems.map(p => getId(p))); } }}
994|              style={{ width: '16px', height: '16px', cursor: 'pointer', accentColor: 'var(--accent)' }} />
995|            <span style={{ fontSize: '13px', color: 'var(--muted)', cursor: 'pointer' }}
996|              onClick={() => { if (selected.length === wishlistItems.length) { setSelected([]); } else { setSelected(wishlistItems.map(p => getId(p))); } }}>
997|              {selected.length === wishlistItems.length && wishlistItems.length > 0 ? 'Deselect all' : 'Select all'}
998|            </span>
999|          </div>
1000|        )}
1001|        {selected.length > 0 && (
1002|          <div style={{ padding: '10px 16px', borderBottom: '1px solid var(--line)' }}>
1003|            <button className="rw-btn rw-btn-pri" style={{ padding: '8px 14px', fontSize: '13px' }}
1004|              onClick={addSelectedToCart}>
1005|              {`Add ${selected.length} to cart`}
1006|            </button>
1007|            <button style={{ marginLeft: '8px', padding: '8px 12px', borderRadius: '8px', border: '1px solid var(--line-2)', background: 'none', cursor: 'pointer', fontSize: '12px', transition: 'all 0.15s' }}
1008|              onMouseOver={e => { e.target.style.background = 'var(--line)'; e.target.style.transform = 'translateY(-1px)'; }}
1009|              onMouseOut={e => { e.target.style.background = 'none'; e.target.style.transform = ''; }}
1010|              onClick={() => setSelected([])}>Cancel</button>
1011|            <button style={{ marginLeft: '8px', padding: '8px 12px', borderRadius: '8px', border: '1px solid var(--accent)', background: 'none', cursor: 'pointer', fontSize: '12px', color: 'var(--accent)', transition: 'all 0.15s' }}
1012|              onMouseOver={e => { e.target.style.background = 'var(--accent)'; e.target.style.color = 'var(--surface)'; e.target.style.transform = 'translateY(-1px)'; }}
1013|              onMouseOut={e => { e.target.style.background = 'none'; e.target.style.color = 'var(--accent)'; e.target.style.transform = ''; }}
1014|              onClick={() => {
1015|                const ids = [...selected];
1016|                setSelected([]);
1017|                // Remove immediately — App.jsx shows an undo toast

1022|        {wishlistItems.length === 0 ? (

1032|                  <input type="checkbox" checked={selected.includes(getId(p))}
1033|                    onChange={() => toggleSelect(getId(p))}

1035|                </div>

1038|                </div>

1|import React, { useState, useEffect, useRef, useCallback } from 'react';

3|const SESSION_KEY = 'rw_chat_session';
4|const OPEN_POLL_MS = 5000;
5|const BADGE_POLL_MS = 30000;
6|const WELCOME = "Hey! Ask us anything about sizing, an item, or your order. We usually reply within a few hours — this isn't 24/7 live support.";
7|
8|function beep() {
9|  try {
10|    const ctx = new (window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext)();
11|    const osc = ctx.createOscillator();
12|    const gain = ctx.createGain();
13|    osc.type = 'sine';
14|    osc.frequency.value = 880;
15|    gain.gain.value = 0.05;
16|    osc.connect(gain);
17|    gain.connect(ctx.destination);
18|    osc.start();
19|    osc.stop(ctx.currentTime + 0.12);
20|  } catch {}
21|}
22|
23|export default function ChatBubble() {
24|  const [open, setOpen] = useState(false);
25|  const [sessionId, setSessionId] = useState(() => {
26|    try { return localStorage.getItem(SESSION_KEY) || null; } catch { return null; }
27|  });
28|  const [messages, setMessages] = useState([]);
29|  const [input, setInput] = useState('');
30|  const [sending, setSending] = useState(false);
31|  const [unread, setUnread] = useState(0);
32|  const [sessionStatus, setSessionStatus] = useState('open');
33|  const [customerEmail, setCustomerEmail] = useState('');
34|  const [showEmailScreen, setShowEmailScreen] = useState(true);
35|  const scrollRef = useRef(null);
36|  const lastCountRef = useRef(0);
37|
38|  const fetchMessages = useCallback(async (markRead) => {
39|    if (!sessionId) return;
40|    try {
41|      const r = await fetch(`/api/chat/messages?session_id=${encodeURIComponent(sessionId)}`);
42|      const d = await r.json();
43|      const msgs = Array.isArray(d.messages) ? d.messages : [];
44|      setMessages(msgs);
45|      setSessionStatus(d.status || 'open');
46|
47|      const unreadAdmin = msgs.filter(m => m.sender === 'admin' && !m.read_by_customer).length;
48|      if (!open) {
49|        if (unreadAdmin > lastCountRef.current) beep();
50|        setUnread(unreadAdmin);
51|      } else if (markRead && unreadAdmin > 0) {
52|        setUnread(0);
53|        fetch('/api/chat/mark-read', {
54|          method: 'POST',
55|          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
56|          body: JSON.stringify({ session_id: sessionId }),
57|        }).catch(() => {});
58|      }
59|      lastCountRef.current = unreadAdmin;
60|    } catch {}
61|  }, [sessionId, open]);
62|
63|  useEffect(() => {
64|    if (!sessionId) return;
65|    const tick = () => { fetchMessages(open); };
66|    tick();
67|    const interval = setInterval(tick, open ? OPEN_POLL_MS : BADGE_POLL_MS);
68|    return () => clearInterval(interval);
69|  }, [sessionId, open, fetchMessages]);
70|
71|  useEffect(() => {
72|    if (open && scrollRef.current) {
73|      scrollRef.current.scrollTop = scrollRef.current.scrollHeight;
74|    }
75|  }, [messages, open]);
76|
77|  async function handleSend() {
78|    const text = input.trim();
79|    if (!text || sending) return;
80|    setSending(true);
81|    setInput('');
82|    try {
83|      if (!sessionId) {
84|        const r = await fetch('/api/chat/start', {
85|          method: 'POST',
86|          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
87|          body: JSON.stringify({ message: text, customer_email: customerEmail || undefined }),
88|        });
89|        const d = await r.json();
90|        if (d.session_id) {
91|          localStorage.setItem(SESSION_KEY, d.session_id);
92|          setSessionId(d.session_id);
93|          setMessages([{ sender: 'customer', message: text, created_at: new Date().toISOString() }]);
94|        }
95|      } else {
96|        setMessages((prev) => [...prev, { sender: 'customer', message: text, created_at: new Date().toISOString() }]);
97|        await fetch('/api/chat/send', {
98|          method: 'POST',
99|          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
100|          body: JSON.stringify({ session_id: sessionId, message: text }),
101|        });
102|        fetchMessages(true);
103|      }
104|    } catch {
105|      setInput(text);
106|    } finally {
107|      setSending(false);
108|    }
109|  }
110|
111|  function handleOpen() {
112|    setOpen(true);
113|    setUnread(0);
114|    if (!sessionId) setShowEmailScreen(true);
115|    if (sessionId) fetchMessages(true);
116|  }
117|
118|  const showGreeting = messages.length === 0;
119|
120|  // Don't render on admin pages
121|  if (typeof window !== 'undefined' && window.location.hash === '#admin') return null;
122|
123|  return (
124|    <div style={{ position: 'fixed', bottom: '20px', right: '20px', zIndex: 10000, fontFamily: 'inherit' }}>
125|      {open && (
126|        <div style={{
127|          width: '360px', height: '480px', background: '#fff', borderRadius: '16px',
128|          boxShadow: '0 8px 30px rgba(0,0,0,.18)', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column',
129|          marginBottom: '12px', overflow: 'hidden', border: '1px solid rgba(0,0,0,.06)',
130|        }}>
131|          <div style={{
132|            padding: '14px 16px', background: 'var(--ink, #16130F)', color: '#fff',
133|            display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center', flexShrink: 0,
134|          }}>
135|            <strong style={{ fontSize: '14px' }}>Chat with REWIND</strong>
136|            <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '6px', alignItems: 'center' }}>
137|              {sessionId && (
138|                <button onClick={() => { localStorage.removeItem(SESSION_KEY); setSessionId(null); setMessages([]); setSessionStatus('open'); setCustomerEmail(''); setShowEmailScreen(true); }}
139|                  style={{ background: 'none', border: '1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.3)', color: '#fff', fontSize: '11px', cursor: 'pointer', borderRadius: '6px', padding: '3px 8px' }}>
140|                  New
141|                </button>
142|              )}
143|              <button onClick={() => setOpen(false)} aria-label="Close chat"
144|                style={{ background: 'none', border: 'none', color: '#fff', fontSize: '18px', cursor: 'pointer', lineHeight: 1 }}>
145|                &times;
146|              </button>
147|            </div>
148|          </div>
149|
150|          <div ref={scrollRef} style={{ flex: 1, overflowY: 'auto', padding: '14px', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: '8px' }}>
151|            {showGreeting && (
152|              <div style={{ fontSize: '13px', color: 'var(--muted, #6E665A)', background: '#FAF6EF', borderRadius: '10px', padding: '10px 12px' }}>
153|                {WELCOME}
154|              </div>
155|            )}
156|            {messages.map((m, i) => (
157|              <div key={i} style={{
158|                alignSelf: m.sender === 'admin' || m.sender === 'ai' ? 'flex-start' : 'flex-end',
159|                background: m.sender === 'admin' || m.sender === 'ai' ? '#F1EEE7' : 'var(--accent, #FF4D14)',
160|                color: m.sender === 'admin' ? '#16130F' : '#fff',
161|                borderRadius: '12px', padding: '8px 12px', fontSize: '13px', maxWidth: '80%',
162|                whiteSpace: 'pre-wrap', wordBreak: 'break-word',
163|              }}>
164|                {m.message}
165|              </div>
166|            ))}
167|          </div>
168|
169|          {sessionStatus === 'closed' ? (
170|            <div style={{ padding: '14px', textAlign: 'center' }}>
171|              <p style={{ fontSize: '13px', color: 'var(--muted)', margin: '0 0 12px' }}>💬 Session closed</p>
172|              <button onClick={() => setOpen(false)}
173|                style={{ padding: '8px 16px', marginRight: '8px', borderRadius: '8px', border: '1px solid var(--line-2)', background: 'var(--surface)', cursor: 'pointer', fontSize: '13px' }}>
174|                Close
175|              </button>
176|              <button onClick={() => { localStorage.removeItem(SESSION_KEY); setSessionId(null); setMessages([]); setSessionStatus('open'); setCustomerEmail(''); setShowEmailScreen(true); }}
177|                style={{ padding: '8px 16px', borderRadius: '8px', border: 'none', background: 'var(--accent)', color: '#fff', cursor: 'pointer', fontSize: '13px' }}>
178|                Open a new one
179|              </button>
180|            </div>
181|          ) : !sessionId && showEmailScreen ? (
182|            <div style={{ padding: '14px' }}>
183|              <p style={{ fontSize: '12px', color: 'var(--muted)', margin: '0 0 8px' }}>Enter your email to start chatting</p>
184|              <input value={customerEmail} onChange={e => setCustomerEmail(e.target.value.slice(0, 200))}
185|                placeholder="your@email.com" type="email"
186|                onKeyDown={(e) => { if (e.key === 'Enter' && customerEmail.includes('@')) setShowEmailScreen(false); }}
187|                style={{ width: '100%', padding: '8px 10px', borderRadius: '8px', border: '1px solid #ddd', fontSize: '13px', boxSizing: 'border-box' }} />
188|              <button onClick={() => { if (customerEmail.includes('@')) setShowEmailScreen(false); }}
189|                disabled={!customerEmail.includes('@')}
190|                style={{ display: 'block', width: '100%', marginTop: '8px', padding: '8px', borderRadius: '8px', border: 'none', background: customerEmail.includes('@') ? 'var(--accent)' : 'var(--line-2)', color: '#fff', cursor: customerEmail.includes('@') ? 'pointer' : 'not-allowed', fontWeight: 600, fontSize: '13px' }}>
191|                Continue
192|              </button>
193|            </div>
194|          ) : (
195|          <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '8px', padding: '10px', borderTop: '1px solid rgba(0,0,0,.06)', flexShrink: 0 }}>

198|              onChange={(e) => setInput(e.target.value.slice(0, 2000))}

202|            />

5|/*

8| * Components:

16|
17|/* ── Referral modal dialog ── */
18|export function ReferralDialog({ open, onClose, userEmail, showToast }) {
19|  const [step, setStep] = useState('generate'); // generate | ready | loading
20|  const [code, setCode] = useState('');
21|  const [shareUrl, setShareUrl] = useState('');
22|  const [usedCount, setUsedCount] = useState(0);
23|  const [maxUses, setMaxUses] = useState(10);
24|  const [status, setStatus] = useState('active');
25|  const [rewards, setRewards] = useState([]);
26|  const [redemptions, setRedemptions] = useState([]);
27|  const [copyFeedback, setCopyFeedback] = useState('');
28|  const [statsLoading, setStatsLoading] = useState(false);
29|  const [generateLoading, setGenerateLoading] = useState(false);
30|  const [error, setError] = useState('');
31|
32|  // Reset when dialog opens
33|  useEffect(() => {
34|    if (open) {
35|      setError('');
36|      setCopyFeedback('');
37|      if (userEmail) {
38|        setStep('loading');
39|        loadStats();
40|      } else {
41|        setStep('generate');
42|      }
43|    }
44|  }, [open, userEmail]);
45|
46|  const loadStats = useCallback(async () => {
47|    setStatsLoading(true);
48|    try {
49|      const r = await fetch(`/api/referral/stats?email=${encodeURIComponent(userEmail)}`);
50|      const d = await r.json();
51|      if (d.code) {
52|        setCode(d.code);
53|        setShareUrl(d.shareUrl || `https://rewind-stores.com?ref=${d.code}`);
54|        setUsedCount(d.usedCount || 0);
55|        setMaxUses(d.maxUses || 10);
56|        setStatus(d.status || 'active');
57|        setRewards(d.rewards || []);
58|        setRedemptions(d.redemptions || []);
59|        setStep('ready');
60|      } else {
61|        setStep('generate');
62|      }
63|    } catch {
64|      setError('Could not load referral data');
65|      setStep('generate');
66|    }
67|    setStatsLoading(false);
68|  }, [userEmail]);
69|
70|  const handleGenerate = useCallback(async () => {
71|    if (!userEmail) return;
72|    setGenerateLoading(true);
73|    setError('');
74|    try {
75|      const r = await fetch('/api/referral/generate', {
76|        method: 'POST',
77|        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
78|        body: JSON.stringify({ email: userEmail }),
79|      });
80|      const d = await r.json();
81|      if (d.code) {
82|        setCode(d.code);
83|        setShareUrl(d.shareUrl || `https://rewind-stores.com?ref=${d.code}`);
84|        setStep('ready');
85|        setUsedCount(d.usedCount || 0);
86|        if (showToast) showToast('🎉 Your referral code is ready! Check your email.');
87|      } else {
88|        setError(d.error || 'Failed to generate code');
89|      }
90|    } catch (e) {
91|      setError('Network error: ' + e.message);
92|    }
93|    setGenerateLoading(false);
94|  }, [userEmail, showToast]);
95|
96|  const handleCopy = useCallback(async (text, label) => {
97|    try {
98|      await navigator.clipboard.writeText(text);
99|      setCopyFeedback(label || 'Copied!');
100|      setTimeout(() => setCopyFeedback(''), 2000);
101|    } catch {
102|      setCopyFeedback('Failed to copy');
103|      setTimeout(() => setCopyFeedback(''), 2000);
104|    }
105|  }, []);
106|
107|  const unclaimedRewards = rewards.filter(r => r.status === 'issued');
108|  const pendingRedemptions = redemptions.filter(r => r.status === 'pending');
109|  const qualifiedRedemptions = redemptions.filter(r => r.status === 'qualified');
110|
111|  if (!open) return null;
112|
113|  const activeRewardCount = unclaimedRewards.length;
114|
115|  return (
116|    <div className="rw-ref-page">
117|      <div className="rw-ref-page-header">
118|        <button className="rw-btn rw-btn-ghost" onClick={onClose} style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '6px' }}>
119|          <Icon name="arrow" size={16} /> Back
120|        </button>
121|      </div>

126|            <p style={{ color: 'var(--muted)' }}>Loading your referral info…</p>
127|          </div>
128|        )}
129|

279|/* ── Inline referral input (for checkout) ── */
280|export function ReferralInput({ onApply, appliedReferral, referralDiscount, referralLoading, referralError }) {
281|  const [code, setCode] = useState('');
282|
283|  useEffect(() => {
284|    if (appliedReferral) setCode('');
285|  }, [appliedReferral]);
286|
287|  const handleApply = () => {
288|    if (!code.trim() || referralLoading) return;
289|    onApply(code.trim());
290|  };
291|
292|  return (
293|    <div className="rw-co-sec">
294|      <h3>Referral code</h3>
295|      <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '8px', alignItems: 'stretch' }}>
296|        <input className="rw-input" placeholder="Enter referral code"
297|          value={code} onChange={e => setCode(e.target.value.toUpperCase())}
298|          disabled={!!appliedReferral}
299|          style={{ marginBottom: 0, flex: 1 }} />
300|        {!appliedReferral ? (
301|          <button className="rw-btn rw-btn-ghost" onClick={handleApply}
302|            disabled={!code.trim() || referralLoading}
303|            style={{ padding: '13px 18px', fontSize: '13px', whiteSpace: 'nowrap', flexShrink: 0 }}>
304|            {referralLoading ? '…' : 'Apply'}
305|          </button>
306|        ) : (
307|          <button className="rw-btn rw-btn-ghost" onClick={() => onApply('')}
308|            style={{ padding: '13px 18px', fontSize: '13px', whiteSpace: 'nowrap', flexShrink: 0, color: 'var(--accent)' }}>
309|            Remove
310|          </button>
311|        )}
312|      </div>
313|      {referralLoading && (
314|        <span style={{ color: 'var(--muted)', fontSize: '13px', marginTop: '6px', display: 'block', fontWeight: 500 }}>
315|          ⏳ Checking…
316|        </span>
317|      )}
318|      {appliedReferral && (
319|        <span style={{ color: '#0E9F6E', fontSize: '13px', marginTop: '6px', display: 'block', fontWeight: 600 }}>
320|          ✓ Referral applied — {referralDiscount}% off!
321|        </span>
322|      )}
323|      {referralError && !appliedReferral && (
324|        <span style={{ color: 'var(--accent)', fontSize: '13px', marginTop: '6px', display: 'block' }}>
325|          {referralError}
326|        </span>
327|      )}
328|      <p style={{ fontSize: '11.5px', color: 'var(--muted)', marginTop: '6px', lineHeight: '1.4' }}>
329|        Have a referral code? Enter it above to get {REFERRAL_DISCOUNT}% off your order.
330|      </p>
331|    </div>
332|  );

65|function getToken() {
66|  try { return localStorage.getItem('rw_admin_token') || ''; } catch { return ''; }
67|}
68|
69|async function apiGet(path) {
70|  const token = getToken();
71|  const r = await fetch(path, {
72|    headers: { 'x-admin-token': token },
73|  });
74|  if (!r.ok) throw new Error(await r.text());
75|  return r.json();
76|}
77|
78|async function apiPost(path, body) {
79|  const token = getToken();
80|  const r = await fetch(path, {
81|    method: 'POST',
82|    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'x-admin-token': token },
83|    body: JSON.stringify(body),
84|  });
85|  if (!r.ok) throw new Error(await r.text());
86|  return r.json();

89|function copyToClipboard(text) {
90|  if (navigator.clipboard) navigator.clipboard.writeText(text).catch(() => {});

94|function Pulse() {
95|  const [data, setData] = useState(null);
96|  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
97|  const [error, setError] = useState(null);
98|
99|  const load = useCallback(async () => {
100|    setLoading(true); setError(null);
101|    try { setData(await apiGet('/api/settings/pulse')); }
102|    catch (e) { setError(e.message); }
103|    setLoading(false);
104|  }, []);
105|
106|  useEffect(() => { load(); }, [load]);
107|
108|  if (loading) return <div style={{ fontSize: '13px', color: 'var(--muted)' }}>Loading pulse…</div>;
109|  if (error) return (
110|    <div>

112|      <button onClick={load} style={SP_STYLES.btnSmall}>Retry</button>
113|    </div>
114|  );
115|  if (!data) return null;
116|
117|  return (
118|    <div>
119|      <div style={SP_STYLES.statRow}>
120|        <div style={SP_STYLES.statBox}>
121|          <p style={SP_STYLES.statValue}>€{data.todaySales.toFixed(2)}</p>

154|function OrderLookup() {
155|  const [q, setQ] = useState('');
156|  const [orders, setOrders] = useState([]);
157|  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
158|  const [searched, setSearched] = useState(false);
159|
160|  const search = useCallback(async () => {
161|    if (!q.trim()) return;
162|    setLoading(true); setSearched(true);
163|    try { setOrders((await apiGet('/api/settings/order-lookup?q=' + encodeURIComponent(q.trim()))).orders || []); }
164|    catch { setOrders([]); }
165|    setLoading(false);
166|  }, [q]);
167|
168|  const statusColor = (s) => {
169|    const m = { paid: '#059669', confirmed: '#059669', pending: '#92400E', cancelled: '#991B1B', payment_failed: '#991B1B', shipped: '#1D4ED8' };
170|    return m[s] || 'var(--muted)';
171|  };
172|
173|  return (
174|    <div>
175|      <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '8px' }}>
176|        <input style={SP_STYLES.input} placeholder="Order number…" value={q} onChange={e => setQ(e.target.value)} onKeyDown={e => { if (e.key === 'Enter') search(); }} />
177|        <button onClick={search} disabled={loading || !q.trim()} style={SP_STYLES.btn}>{loading ? '…' : 'Search'}</button>
178|      </div>
179|      {orders.length === 0 && searched && <p style={{ fontSize: '13px', color: 'var(--muted)', marginTop: '12px', textAlign: 'center' }}>No orders found</p>}
180|      {orders.map((o, i) => (
181|        <div key={o.order_num || i} style={{ marginTop: '12px', padding: '14px', borderRadius: '10px', background: 'var(--bg)', border: '1px solid var(--line)' }}>
182|          <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center', marginBottom: '6px' }}>
183|            <span style={{ fontWeight: 700, fontSize: '14px', color: 'var(--ink)' }}>{o.order_num}</span>
184|            <span style={{ ...SP_STYLES.tag, background: statusColor(o.status) + '18', color: statusColor(o.status) }}>{o.status}</span>
185|          </div>
186|          <p style={{ fontSize: '12px', color: 'var(--muted)', margin: '0 0 4px' }}>{o.customer_name || '—'} · {o.email || '—'}</p>
187|          <p style={{ fontSize: '12px', color: 'var(--muted)', margin: '0' }}>{Array.isArray(o.items) ? o.items.map(it => it.name || it.product_id || 'Item').join(', ') : '—'}</p>
188|          <p style={{ fontSize: '13px', fontWeight: 600, color: 'var(--ink)', margin: '6px 0 0' }}>€{parseFloat(o.total || 0).toFixed(2)}</p>

195|function PromoGenerator({ showToast }) {
196|  const [discount, setDiscount] = useState(10);
197|  const [generated, setGenerated] = useState(null);
198|  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
199|  const [copied, setCopied] = useState(false);
200|
201|  const generate = useCallback(async () => {
202|    setLoading(true); setGenerated(null); setCopied(false);
203|    try {
204|      const d = await apiPost('/api/settings/generate-promo', { discount });
205|      setGenerated(d);
206|      if (showToast) showToast('Promo code generated!', null, 2000);
207|    } catch (e) {
208|      if (showToast) showToast('Failed: ' + e.message, null, 2500);
209|    }
210|    setLoading(false);
211|  }, [discount, showToast]);
212|
213|  const handleCopy = useCallback(() => {
214|    if (!generated) return;
215|    copyToClipboard(generated.code);
216|    setCopied(true);
217|    if (showToast) showToast('Copied!', null, 1500);
218|    setTimeout(() => setCopied(false), 2000);
219|  }, [generated, showToast]);
220|
221|  return (
222|    <div>
223|      <div style={{ marginBottom: '14px' }}>
224|        <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: '12px', marginBottom: '8px' }}>
225|          <span style={{ fontSize: '13px', fontWeight: 500, color: 'var(--ink)', minWidth: '60px' }}>{discount}%</span>
226|          <input type="range" min="5" max="50" step="5" value={discount} onChange={e => setDiscount(Number(e.target.value))} style={{ flex: 1, accentColor: 'var(--accent, #FF4D14)' }} />
227|        </div>
228|        <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: '6px', fontSize: '11px', color: 'var(--muted)', justifyContent: 'space-between' }}>
229|          <span>5%</span><span>25%</span><span>50%</span>
230|        </div>
231|      </div>
232|      <button onClick={generate} disabled={loading} style={SP_STYLES.btn}>{loading ? 'Generating…' : 'Generate code'}</button>
233|      {generated && (
234|        <div style={{ marginTop: '14px', padding: '12px 14px', borderRadius: '10px', background: 'var(--bg)', border: '1px solid var(--line)', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'space-between' }}>
235|          <div>
236|            <span style={{ fontSize: '16px', fontWeight: 700, color: 'var(--ink)', letterSpacing: '0.5px' }}>{generated.code}</span>
237|            <p style={{ fontSize: '11px', color: 'var(--muted)', margin: '2px 0 0' }}>{discount}% off</p>
238|          </div>
239|          <button onClick={handleCopy} style={SP_STYLES.btnSmall}>{copied ? '✓ Copied' : 'Copy'}</button>
240|        </div>
241|      )}
