340|// Admin: create a promo code (stored in DB)
341|app.post('/api/admin/create-promo', requireAdmin, async (req, res) => {
342|  const { discount, label, code } = req.body;
343|  if (!discount || discount < 1 || discount > 100) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Discount must be 1-100' });
344|  const promoCode = code || 'REWIND-' + Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, 6).toUpperCase();
345|  const SERVICE_KEY = process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY;
346|  try {
347|    const promoRes = await fetch(`${SUPABASE_URL}/rest/v1/promo_codes`, {
348|      method: 'POST',
349|      headers: { apikey: *** Authorization: *** ${SERVICE_KEY}`, 'Content-Type': 'application/json', Prefer: 'return=minimal' },
350|      body: JSON.stringify({ code: promoCode, discount, label: label || `${discount}% off`, created_by: 'admin' }),
351|    });
352|    if (!promoRes.ok) {
353|      const errText = await promoRes.text();
354|      return res.status(500).json({ error: 'Supabase error: ' + errText });
355|    }
356|    res.json({ code: promoCode, discount });

371|    });
372|    res.json({ ok: true });
373|  } else if (action === 'remove') {
374|    await fetch(`${process.env.SUPABASE_URL}/rest/v1/admins?email=eq.${encodeURIComponent(email)}`, {
375|      method: 'DELETE', headers: { apikey: *** Authorization: *** ${SERVICE_KEY}` },
376|    });

378|  } else {
379|    res.status(400).json({ error: 'Invalid action' });

383|// ── Stripe Checkout Session ──
384|app.post('/api/create-checkout-session', async (req, res) => {
385|  if (!stripe) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'STRIPE_SECRET_KEY not configured on Railway' });
386|  const { items, total, orderNum, email, name, address } = req.body;
387|  // Check if email is blocked
388|  try {
389|    const br = await fetch(`${SUPABASE_URL}/rest/v1/blocked_emails?email=eq.${encodeURIComponent(email)}`, {
390|      headers: { apikey: *** Authorization: *** ${SUPABASE_KEY}` }
391|    });
392|    const bd = await br.json();
393|    if (Array.isArray(bd) && bd.length > 0) return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Email is blocked' });
394|  } catch {}
395|  try {
396|    // Look up real prices server-side — never trust the client-supplied price.
397|    const line_items = [];
398|    const productIds = [];
399|    for (const it of (items || [])) {
400|      const pid = it.id || it.product_id;
401|      const realPrice = pid ? await lookupProductPrice(pid) : null;
402|      if (realPrice === null) {
403|        return res.status(400).json({ error: `Unknown product: ${it.name || pid}` });
404|      }
405|      productIds.push(pid);
406|      line_items.push({
407|        price_data: {
408|          currency: 'eur',
409|          product_data: { name: `${it.name}${it.size ? ` (${it.size})` : ''}` },
410|          unit_amount: Math.round(realPrice * 100),
411|        },
412|        quantity: it.qty || 1,
413|      });
414|    }
415|    // Calculate subtotal from server-looked-up prices — never trust client-supplied prices
416|    const realSubtotal = line_items.reduce((s, li) => {
417|      return s + (li.price_data.unit_amount / 100) * li.quantity;
418|    }, 0);
419|    const shipping = realSubtotal >= 15000 ? 0 : 800; // 800 cents = €8
420|    if (shipping > 0) {
421|      line_items.push({
422|        price_data: {
423|          currency: 'eur',
424|          product_data: { name: 'Shipping' },
425|          unit_amount: shipping,
426|        },
427|        quantity: 1,
428|      });
429|    }
430|    if ((items || []).length === 0) {
431|      return res.status(400).json({ error: 'No items in order' });
432|    }
433|    const session = await stripe.checkout.sessions.create({
434|      mode: 'payment',
435|      line_items,
436|      customer_email: email,
437|      metadata: {
438|        orderNum,
439|        customer_name: name || '',
440|        address: address || '',
441|        product_ids: productIds.join(','),
442|      },
443|      success_url: `${process.env.BASE_URL || 'https://rewind-stores.com'}?order=success&orderNum=${orderNum}`,
444|      cancel_url: `${process.env.BASE_URL || 'https://rewind-stores.com'}?order=cancelled`,
445|      payment_method_types: ['card'],
446|    });
447|    res.json({ url: session.url });
448|  } catch (err) {
449|    console.error('Stripe session error:', err);
450|    res.status(500).json({ error: err.message });
451|  }
452|});
453|
454|// Compute real order total server-side — never trust the client
455|async function computeOrder(items, promoCode) {
456|  let subtotal = 0;
457|  for (const it of (items || [])) {
458|    const pid = it.id || it.product_id;
459|    const realPrice = pid ? await lookupProductPrice(pid) : null;
460|    subtotal += (realPrice ?? it.price ?? 0) * (it.qty || 1);
461|  }
462|  const shipping = subtotal >= 150 ? 0 : 8;
463|  let discountPrice = subtotal;
464|  let discountLabel = null;
465|  // Validate promo code against DB
466|  if (promoCode) {
467|    try {
468|      const key = process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY;
469|      const r = await fetch(`${process.env.SUPABASE_URL || 'https://luiqimsfvllgsmzedncw.supabase.co'}/rest/v1/promo_codes?code=eq.${encodeURIComponent(promoCode)}&select=discount,discount_type,label,uses,max_uses`, {
470|        headers: { apikey: *** Authorization: *** ${key}` },
471|      });
472|      const data = await r.json();
473|      if (Array.isArray(data) && data.length > 0) {
474|        const promo = data[0];
475|        if (promo.max_uses == null || (promo.uses || 0) < promo.max_uses) {
476|          if (promo.discount_type === 'free_shipping') {
477|            discountPrice = subtotal;
478|            discountLabel = 'Free shipping';
479|          } else {
480|            discountPrice = Math.round(subtotal * (100 - promo.discount)) / 100;
481|            discountLabel = `${promo.discount}% off`;
482|          }
483|        }
484|      }
485|    } catch {}
486|  }
487|  return { subtotal, shipping, discountPrice, discountLabel };
488|}
489|
490|// Decrement custom_products.stock for a paid order's line items (by product id).
491|// Shared by both the legacy checkout.session.completed path and the live
492|// payment_intent.succeeded path so stock actually depletes on real orders.
493|async function decrementStockByIds(items) {
494|  const key = process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY;
495|  const url = process.env.VITE_SUPABASE_URL || SUPABASE_URL;
496|  if (!key || !url) return;
497|  for (const it of (items || [])) {
498|    const pid = it.id || it.product_id;
499|    const qty = it.qty || 1;
500|    if (!pid) continue;
501|    try {
502|      const r = await fetch(`${url}/rest/v1/custom_products?product_id=eq.${encodeURIComponent(pid)}`, {
503|        headers: { apikey: *** Authorization: *** ${key}` },
504|      });
505|      const products = await r.json();
506|      if (!Array.isArray(products) || products.length === 0) continue;
507|      const p = products[0];
508|      const currentStock = p.stock ?? 0;
509|      const newStock = Math.max(0, currentStock - qty);
510|      await fetch(`${url}/rest/v1/custom_products?id=eq.${p.id}`, {
511|        method: 'PATCH',
512|        headers: { apikey: *** Authorization: *** ${key}`, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
513|        body: JSON.stringify({ stock: newStock }),
514|      });
515|    } catch (e) {
516|      console.warn(`Stock decrement failed for "${pid}":`, e.message);
517|    }
518|  }
519|}

521|// ── Stripe Payment Intent (for Elements) ──
522|app.post('/api/create-payment-intent', async (req, res) => {
523|  if (!stripe) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'STRIPE_SECRET_KEY not configured' });
524|  const { items, orderNum, email, name, address, promoCode } = req.body;
525|  if (!items || !items.length || !orderNum || !email) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Missing required fields' });
526|  // Server-side price recompute — never trust client amounts
527|  const { subtotal, discountPrice } = await computeOrder(items, promoCode);
528|  const finalTotal = Math.round(discountPrice * 100);
529|  try {
530|    const paymentIntent = await stripe.paymentIntents.create({
531|      amount: finalTotal,
532|      currency: 'eur',
533|      metadata: { orderNum, email, name: name || '', address: (address || '').slice(0, 480), itemsJson: JSON.stringify(items.map(i => ({ id: i.id, qty: i.qty, price: i.price }))), promoCode: promoCode || '' },
534|      payment_method_types: ['card'],
535|    });
536|    res.json({ clientSecret: paymentIntent.client_secret });
537|  } catch (e) {
538|    console.error('PaymentIntent error:', e);
539|    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Could not create payment: ' + e.message });
540|  }
541|});

606|// Stripe webhook — save order on payment success
607|app.post('/api/stripe-webhook', async (req, res) => {
608|  const sig = req.headers['stripe-signature'];
609|  let event;
610|  try {
611|    event = stripe.webhooks.constructEvent(req.rawBody, sig, process.env.STRIPE_WEBHOOK_SECRET);
612|  } catch (err) {
613|    return res.status(400).send(`Webhook Error: ${err.message}`);
614|  }
615|  if (event.type === 'checkout.session.completed') {
616|    const session = event.data.object;
617|    const { orderNum, customer_name, address } = session.metadata || {};
618|    const email = session.customer_details?.email || session.customer_email || '';
619|    try {
620|      const lineItems = await stripe.checkout.sessions.listLineItems(session.id);
621|      const items = lineItems.data.map(it => ({ name: it.description, price: it.amount_total / 100, qty: it.quantity }));
622|      const total = session.amount_total / 100;
623|      // Save order to Supabase
624|      await fetch(`${process.env.SUPABASE_URL || SUPABASE_URL}/rest/v1/orders`, {
625|        method: 'POST',
626|        headers: { apikey: proces..._KEY || SUPABASE_KEY, Authorization: *** ${process.env.SUPABASE_KEY || SUPABASE_KEY}`, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
627|        body: JSON.stringify({
628|          order_num: orderNum, customer_name, email, address: address || '',
629|          items: Array.isArray(items) ? JSON.stringify(items) : '[]',
630|          total, status: 'paid',
631|        }),
632|      });
633|      // Decrement stock for purchased items — use product_ids from metadata if available
634|      const productIds = session.metadata?.product_ids ? session.metadata.product_ids.split(',').filter(Boolean) : [];
635|      if (productIds.length > 0 && productIds.length === items.length) {
636|        for (let i = 0; i < productIds.length; i++) {
637|          const pid = productIds[i];
638|          const qty = items[i]?.qty || 1;
639|          if (!pid) continue;
640|          const res = await fetch(`${process.env.SUPABASE_URL || SUPABASE_URL}/rest/v1/custom_products?product_id=eq.${encodeURIComponent(pid)}`, {
641|            headers: { apikey: proces..._KEY || SUPABASE_KEY, Authorization: *** ${process.env.SUPABASE_KEY || SUPABASE_KEY}` },
642|          });
643|          const products = await res.json();
644|          if (!products || products.length === 0) {
645|            console.warn(`Webhook: no custom_product found for product_id "${pid}" — skipping stock decrement`);
646|            continue;
647|          }
648|          const p = products[0];
649|          const currentStock = p.stock ?? 0;
650|          if (qty > currentStock) {
651|            console.warn(`Webhook: insufficient stock for "${pid}" (have ${currentStock}, need ${qty}) — clamping to 0`);
652|          }
653|          const newStock = Math.max(0, currentStock - qty);
654|          await fetch(`${process.env.SUPABASE_URL || SUPABASE_URL}/rest/v1/custom_products?id=eq.${p.id}`, {
655|            method: 'PATCH',
656|            headers: { apikey: proces..._KEY || SUPABASE_KEY, Authorization: *** ${process.env.SUPABASE_KEY || SUPABASE_KEY}`, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
657|            body: JSON.stringify({ stock: newStock }),
658|          });
659|        }
660|      } else {
661|        for (const it of items) {
662|          if (!it.name || !it.qty) continue;
663|          const productName = it.name.replace(/\s*\(.*?\)\s*$/, '').trim();
664|          const res = await fetch(`${process.env.SUPABASE_URL || SUPABASE_URL}/rest/v1/custom_products?name=eq.${encodeURIComponent(productName)}`, {
665|            headers: { apikey: proces..._KEY || SUPABASE_KEY, Authorization: *** ${process.env.SUPABASE_KEY || SUPABASE_KEY}` },
666|          });
667|          const products = await res.json();
668|          if (!products || products.length === 0) {
669|            console.warn(`Webhook: no custom_product found for "${productName}" — skipping stock decrement`);
670|            continue;
671|          }
672|          const p = products[0];
673|          const currentStock = p.stock ?? 0;
674|          if (it.qty > currentStock) {
675|            console.warn(`Webhook: insufficient stock for "${productName}" (have ${currentStock}, need ${it.qty}) — clamping to 0`);
676|          }
677|          const newStock = Math.max(0, currentStock - it.qty);
678|          await fetch(`${process.env.SUPABASE_URL || SUPABASE_URL}/rest/v1/custom_products?id=eq.${p.id}`, {
679|            method: 'PATCH',
680|            headers: { apikey: proces..._KEY || SUPABASE_KEY, Authorization: *** ${process.env.SUPABASE_KEY || SUPABASE_KEY}`, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
681|            body: JSON.stringify({ stock: newStock }),
682|          });
683|        }
684|      }
685|      if (process.env.RESEND_API_KEY) {
686|        await fetch(`http://localhost:${PORT}/api/send-order`, {
687|          method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
688|          body: JSON.stringify({ email, name: customer_name, items, total, address, orderNum }),
689|        });
690|      }
691|    } catch (e) { console.error('Webhook error:', e); }
692|  }
693|
694|  // Handle payment failures — mark order as failed in Supabase
695|  if (event.type === 'payment_intent.succeeded') {
696|    const pi = event.data.object;
697|    const { orderNum, email, name, address, itemsJson, promoCode } = pi.metadata || {};
698|    if (orderNum && email) {
699|      try {
700|        const items = itemsJson ? JSON.parse(itemsJson) : [];
701|        const { subtotal, shipping, discountPrice } = await computeOrder(items, promoCode);
702|        const total = discountPrice + shipping;
703|        await fetch(`${SUPABASE_URL}/rest/v1/orders`, {
704|          method: 'POST',
705|          headers: { apikey: *** Authorization: *** ${SERVICE_KEY}`, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
706|          body: JSON.stringify({ order_num: orderNum, email, customer_name: name || '', address: address || '', items: JSON.stringify(items), total, shipping, status: 'confirmed', created_at: new Date().toISOString() }),
707|        });
708|        console.log('Order saved from PaymentIntent:', orderNum);
709|
710|        // Decrement stock — this is the live checkout path, so this is the
711|        // only place real orders actually deplete inventory.
712|        await decrementStockByIds(items);
713|
714|        // Send the customer's order-confirmation email (previously only the
715|        // legacy checkout.session.completed path did this — the live
716|        // Stripe Elements flow silently never emailed customers).
717|        if (process.env.RESEND_API_KEY) {
718|          const internalToken = process.env.ADMIN_API_TOKEN || process.env.ADMIN_SECRET_TOKEN || '';
719|          fetch(`http://localhost:${PORT}/api/send-order`, {
720|            method: 'POST',
721|            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'x-internal-token': internalToken },
722|            body: JSON.stringify({ email, name, items, total, address, orderNum }),
723|          }).catch((e) => console.warn('send-order call failed:', e.message));
724|        }
725|
726|        // Check for pending referral redemption and fulfill it
727|        try {
728|          const refUrl = `http://localhost:${PORT}/api/referral/fulfill`;
729|          const INTERNAL_TOKEN = process.env.ADMIN_API_TOKEN || process.env.ADMIN_SECRET_TOKEN;
730|          await fetch(refUrl, {
731|            method: 'POST',
732|            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json', 'x-internal-token': INTERNAL_TOKEN || '' },
733|            body: JSON.stringify({ orderNum }),
734|          });
735|        } catch (refErr) {
736|          console.warn('Referral fulfill failed:', refErr.message);
737|        }
738|      } catch (e) { console.error('Failed to fulfill from PaymentIntent:', e); }
739|    }
740|  }
741|  if (event.type === 'checkout.session.expired' || event.type === 'payment_intent.payment_failed') {
742|    const session = event.data.object;
743|    const orderNum = session.metadata?.orderNum;
744|    if (orderNum) {
745|      try {
746|        const key = process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY;
747|        if (SUPABASE_URL && key) {
748|          await fetch(`${SUPABASE_URL}/rest/v1/orders?order_num=eq.${encodeURIComponent(orderNum)}`, {
749|            method: 'PATCH',
750|            headers: { apikey: *** Authorization: *** ${key}`, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
751|            body: JSON.stringify({ status: 'payment_failed' }),
752|          });
753|        }
754|      } catch {}
755|    }
756|  }
757|
758|  res.json({ received: true });
759|});

827|// ── Admin: block a chat customer (email + IP) ──
828|app.post('/api/admin/block-customer', express.json(), async (req, res) => {
829|  const { session_id, email, ip } = req.body;
830|  if (!session_id && !email) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'session_id or email required' });
831|  const SERVICE_KEY = process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY;
832|  if (!SERVICE_KEY) return res.status(500).json({ error: 'Supabase not configured' });
833|
834|  // If session_id given, look up the session to get email and IP
835|  let targetEmail = email;
836|  let targetIp = ip;
837|  if (session_id && (!targetEmail || !targetIp)) {
838|    try {
839|      const r = await fetch(`${SUPABASE_URL}/rest/v1/chat_sessions?session_id=eq.${encodeURIComponent(session_id)}&select=customer_email,customer_ip`, {
840|        headers: { apikey: proces...KEY, Authorization: *** ${process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY}` },
841|      });
842|      const data = await r.json();
843|      if (Array.isArray(data) && data.length > 0) {
844|        if (!targetEmail && data[0].customer_email) targetEmail = data[0].customer_email;
845|        if (!targetIp && data[0].customer_ip) targetIp = data[0].customer_ip;
846|      }
847|    } catch (e) { console.warn('Failed to look up session for blocking:', e.message); }
848|  }
849|
850|  const results = { emailBlocked: false, ipBlocked: false };
851|  const errors = [];
852|
853|  // Block email
854|  if (targetEmail) {
855|    try {
856|      const r = await fetch(`${SUPABASE_URL}/rest/v1/blocked_emails`, {
857|        method: 'POST',
858|        headers: { apikey: proces...KEY, Authorization: *** ${process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY}`, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
859|        body: JSON.stringify({ email: targetEmail.toLowerCase().trim(), created_at: new Date().toISOString() }),
860|      });
861|      if (r.ok) {
862|        BLOCKED_EMAILS.add(targetEmail.toLowerCase().trim());
863|        results.emailBlocked = true;
864|      } else {
865|        const e = await r.json();
866|        if (e.error && !e.error.includes('duplicate')) errors.push('Email: ' + e.error);
867|      }
868|    } catch (e) { errors.push('Email: ' + e.message); }
869|  }
870|
871|  // Block IP
872|  if (targetIp) {
873|    try {
874|      const r = await fetch(`${SUPABASE_URL}/rest/v1/blocked_ips`, {
875|        method: 'POST',
876|        headers: { apikey: proces...KEY, Authorization: *** ${process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY}`, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
877|        body: JSON.stringify({ ip_address: targetIp, created_at: new Date().toISOString() }),
878|      });
879|      if (r.ok) {
880|        BLOCKED_IPS.set(targetIp, true);
881|        results.ipBlocked = true;
882|      } else {
883|        const e = await r.json();
884|        if (e.error && !e.error.includes('duplicate')) errors.push('IP: ' + e.error);
885|      }
886|    } catch (e) { errors.push('IP: ' + e.message); }
887|  }
888|
889|  res.json({ ok: results.emailBlocked || results.ipBlocked, ...results, errors: errors.length > 0 ? errors : undefined });
890|});

892|app.post('/api/admin/unblock-email', express.json(), async (req, res) => {
893|  const { email } = req.body;
894|  if (!email) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Email required' });
895|  try {
896|    const r = await fetch(`${SUPABASE_URL}/rest/v1/blocked_emails?email=eq.${encodeURIComponent(email.toLowerCase().trim())}`, { method: 'DELETE', headers: { apikey: proces...KEY, Authorization: *** ${process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY}` } });
897|    const d = await r.json();
898|    if (d.error) return res.status(500).json({ error: d.error });
899|    res.json({ ok: true });
900|  } catch (e) { res.status(500).json({ error: e.message }); }
901|});

905|  try {
906|    const [ords, wls] = await Promise.all([
907|      fetch(`${SUPABASE_URL}/rest/v1/orders?select=email`, { headers: { apikey: *** Authorization: *** ${SUPABASE_KEY}` } }).then(r => r.json()),
908|      fetch(`${SUPABASE_URL}/rest/v1/wishlists?select=email`, { headers: { apikey: *** Authorization: *** ${SUPABASE_KEY}` } }).then(r => r.json()),
909|    ]);
910|    const emailSet = new Set();
911|    (Array.isArray(ords) ? ords : []).forEach(o => { if (o.email) emailSet.add(o.email.toLowerCase().trim()); });
912|    (Array.isArray(wls) ? wls : []).forEach(w => { if (w.email) emailSet.add(w.email.toLowerCase().trim()); });
913|    res.json({ emails: [...emailSet].sort() });
914|  } catch { res.json({ emails: [] }); }
915|});

959|app.post('/api/admin/products/upload-image', requireAdmin, async (req, res) => {
960|  const SERVICE_KEY = process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY;
961|  if (!SERVICE_KEY || !SUPABASE_URL) return res.status(500).json({ error: 'Supabase not configured' });
962|  try {
963|    const { productId, imageBase64, ext } = req.body;
964|    if (!productId || !imageBase64) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'productId and imageBase64 required' });
965|    const buf = Buffer.from(imageBase64, 'base64');
966|    const allowed = ['jpg','jpeg','png','webp'];
967|    const fileExt = ext && allowed.includes(ext) ? ext : 'webp';
968|    const filePath = `${productId}.${fileExt}`;
969|    const r = await fetch(`${SUPABASE_URL}/storage/v1/object/product-images/${filePath}`, {
970|      method: 'POST',
971|      headers: { apikey: *** Authorization: *** ${SERVICE_KEY}`, 'Content-Type': 'application/octet-stream', 'x-upsert': 'true' },
972|      body: buf,
973|    });
974|    if (!r.ok) return res.status(500).json({ error: 'Upload failed' });
975|    const publicUrl = `${SUPABASE_URL}/storage/v1/object/public/product-images/${filePath}`;
976|    res.json({ ok: true, url: publicUrl });
977|  } catch (e) { res.status(500).json({ error: e.message }); }
978|});

995|// ── Admin: preview cancellation email (generates text without sending) ──
996|app.post('/api/admin/preview-cancel-email', requireAdmin, async (req, res) => {
997|  const { reason, customReason, customerName } = req.body;
998|  const reasonLabels = { out_of_stock: 'Out of stock', damaged: 'Damaged during handling', customer_request: 'Customer requested cancellation', other: 'Other' };
999|  const reasonText = reason === 'other' && customReason ? customReason : (reasonLabels[reason] || reason);
1000|  let emailBody = '';
1001|  const cannedEmails = {
1002|    out_of_stock: `Hi ${customerName || 'there'},\n\nWe regret to inform you that your recent REWIND order has been cancelled due to the item being out of stock. A full refund has been initiated and will appear in your account within 5-10 business days. If you have any questions, reply to this email or contact us at orders@rewind-stores.com.\n\n— REWIND team`,
1003|    damaged: `Hi ${customerName || 'there'},\n\nWe regret to inform you that your recent REWIND order has been cancelled because the item was damaged during handling. A full refund has been initiated and will appear in your account within 5-10 business days. If you have any questions, reply to this email or contact us at orders@rewind-stores.com.\n\n— REWIND team`,
1004|    customer_request: `Hi ${customerName || 'there'},\n\nAs requested, your recent REWIND order has been cancelled. A full refund has been initiated and will appear in your account within 5-10 business days. If you have any questions, reply to this email or contact us at orders@rewind-stores.com.\n\n— REWIND team`,
1005|  };
1006|
1007|  if (reason !== 'other' && cannedEmails[reason]) {
1008|    emailBody = cannedEmails[reason];
1009|  } else {
1010|    const aiRes = await fetch(`https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/models/gemini-2.5-flash:generateContent?key=${process.env.GEMINI_API_KEY}`, {
1011|      method: 'POST',
1012|      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
1013|      body: JSON.stringify({
1014|        contents: [{
1015|          parts: [{
1016|            text: `Write a cancellation email for a REWIND vintage streetwear order. The customer's name is ${customerName || 'there'}. The reason is: "${reasonText}". Use this exact structure:
1017|
1018|            1. Greeting: "Hi [customer name],"
1019|            2. One sentence stating the cancellation and the specific reason
1020|            3. "A full refund has been initiated and will appear in your account within 5-10 business days."
1021|            4. "If you have any questions, reply to this email or contact us at orders@rewind-stores.com."
1022|            5. Sign-off: "— REWIND team"
1023|
1024|            Keep it concise and professional. No slang, no emoji, no exclamation marks. Max 5 short sentences. No subject line.`
1025|          }]
1026|        }],
1027|        generationConfig: { maxOutputTokens: 2000 },
1028|      }),
1029|    });
1030|    const aiData = await aiRes.json();
1031|    emailBody = aiData?.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts?.[0]?.text || '';
1032|  }
1033|  if (!emailBody) {
1034|    const fallbacks = {
1035|      out_of_stock: "Unfortunately, the item you ordered is out of stock and we're unable to fulfill it.",
1036|      damaged: "Unfortunately, the item was damaged during handling and we cannot send it out.",
1037|      customer_request: "You requested cancellation of this order.",
1038|      other: "Your order has been cancelled as requested.",
1039|    };
1040|    emailBody = fallbacks[reason] || 'Your order has been cancelled.';
1041|    if (reason === 'other' && customReason) emailBody = customReason;
1042|  }
1043|  res.json({ emailBody, reasonText });
1044|});

1046|// ── Admin: cancel order ──
1047|app.post('/api/admin/cancel-order', requireAdmin, async (req, res) => {
1048|  const { orderId, reason, customReason } = req.body;
1049|  if (!orderId || !reason) return res.status(400).json({ error: 'orderId and reason required' });
1050|  try {
1051|    // Update order status
1052|    const SERVICE_KEY = process.env.SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY;
1053|    const r = await fetch(`${SUPABASE_URL}/rest/v1/orders?id=eq.${orderId}`, {
1054|      method: 'PATCH',
1055|      headers: { apikey: *** Authorization: *** ${SERVICE_KEY}`, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
1056|      body: JSON.stringify({ status: 'cancelled' }),
1057|    });
1058|    if (!r.ok) {
1059|      const errBody = await r.text();
1060|      console.error('Supabase PATCH failed:', errBody);
1061|      return res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to update order in database. Check server logs.' });
1062|    }
1063|    // Fetch order details for the email
1064|    const orderData = await fetch(`${SUPABASE_URL}/rest/v1/orders?id=eq.${orderId}`, {
1065|      headers: { apikey: *** Authorization: *** ${SERVICE_KEY}` },
1066|    }).then(r => r.json());
1067|    const order = Array.isArray(orderData) ? orderData[0] : null;
1068|    // Send cancellation email
1069|    if (order?.email && resend) {
1070|      const reasonLabels = { out_of_stock: 'Out of stock', damaged: 'Damaged during handling', customer_request: 'Customer requested cancellation', other: 'Other' };
1071|      // Use canned emails for predefined reasons, AI for "Other"
1072|      let emailBody = '';
1073|      const reasonText = reason === 'other' && customReason ? customReason : (reasonLabels[reason] || reason);
1074|      const cannedEmails = {
1075|        out_of_stock: `Hi ${order.customer_name || 'there'},\n\nWe regret to inform you that your recent REWIND order has been cancelled due to the item being out of stock. A full refund has been initiated and will appear in your account within 5-10 business days. If you have any questions, reply to this email or contact us at orders@rewind-stores.com.\n\n— REWIND team`,
1076|        damaged: `Hi ${order.customer_name || 'there'},\n\nWe regret to inform you that your recent REWIND order has been cancelled because the item was damaged during handling. A full refund has been initiated and will appear in your account within 5-10 business days. If you have any questions, reply to this email or contact us at orders@rewind-stores.com.\n\n— REWIND team`,
1077|        customer_request: `Hi ${order.customer_name || 'there'},\n\nAs requested, your recent REWIND order has been cancelled. A full refund has been initiated and will appear in your account within 5-10 business days. If you have any questions, reply to this email or contact us at orders@rewind-stores.com.\n\n— REWIND team`,
1078|      };
1079|      if (reason !== 'other' && cannedEmails[reason]) {
1080|        emailBody = cannedEmails[reason];
1081|      } else {
1082|        try {
1083|          const aiRes = await fetch(`https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/models/gemini-2.5-flash:generateContent?key=${process.env.GEMINI_API_KEY}`, {
1084|            method: 'POST',
1085|            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
1086|            body: JSON.stringify({
1087|              contents: [{
1088|                parts: [{
1089|                  text: `Write a cancellation email for a REWIND vintage streetwear order. The customer's name is ${order.customer_name || 'there'}. The reason is: "${reasonText}". Use this exact structure:\n\n1. Greeting: "Hi [customer name],"\n2. One sentence stating the cancellation and the specific reason\n3. "A full refund has been initiated and will appear in your account within 5-10 business days."\n4. "If you have any questions, reply to this email or contact us at orders@rewind-stores.com."\n5. Sign-off: "— REWIND team"\n\nKeep it concise and professional. No slang, no emoji, no exclamation marks. Max 5 short sentences. No subject line.`
1090|                }]
1091|              }],
1092|              generationConfig: { maxOutputTokens: 2000 },
1093|            }),
1094|          });
1095|          const aiData = await aiRes.json();
1096|          emailBody = aiData?.candidates?.[0]?.content?.parts?.[0]?.text || '';
1097|        } catch {}
1098|      }
1099|      if (!emailBody) {
1100|        // Fallback if AI fails
1101|        const fallbacks = {
1102|          out_of_stock: "Unfortunately, the item you ordered is out of stock and we're unable to fulfill it.",
1103|          damaged: "Unfortunately, the item was damaged during handling and we cannot send it out.",
1104|          customer_request: "You requested cancellation of this order.",
1105|          other: "Your order has been cancelled as requested.",
1106|        };
1107|        emailBody = fallbacks[reason] || 'Your order has been cancelled.';
1108|        if (reason === 'other' && customReason) emailBody = customReason;
1109|      }
1110|      await resend.emails.send({
1111|        from: FROM_EMAIL, reply_to: REPLY_TO, to: order.email,
1112|        subject: `Order ${order.order_num} cancelled — refund initiated`,
1113|        html: `<div style="font-family:sans-serif;max-width:560px;margin:0 auto;padding:40px 20px;background:#FAF6EF">
1114|          <h1 style="font-size:24px;color:#16130F">REWIND<span style="color:#FF4D14">.</span></h1>
1115|          <div style="background:#fff;border-radius:14px;padding:32px;margin-top:20px">
1116|            <h2 style="font-size:20px;color:#16130F;margin:0 0 8px">Order cancelled</h2>
1117|            <p style="color:#6E665A;font-size:15px;line-height:1.6">Hi ${order.customer_name || 'there'},</p>
1118|            <p style="color:#6E665A;font-size:15px;line-height:1.6">
1119|              ${emailBody}<br/><br/>
1120|              <b>Reason:</b> ${reasonText}<br/><br/>
1121|              If you have any questions, reply to this email or contact us at orders@rewind-stores.com.
1122|            </p>
1123|            <p style="color:#6E665A;font-size:14px;margin-top:20px">— REWIND team</p>
1124|          </div>
1125|        </div>`,
1126|      });
1127|    }
1128|    res.json({ ok: true });
1129|  } catch (err) {
1130|    console.error('Cancel order error:', err);
1131|    res.status(500).json({ error: err.message });
1132|  }

32|// Small reusable component — defined outside App() to prevent TDZ issues with
33|// the minifier reordering hoisted function declarations before state variables.
34|function SidebarBtn({ label, isOn, onClick, count }) {
35|  return (
36|    <button className={"rw-sb-btn" + (isOn ? " is-on" : "")} onClick={onClick}>
37|      <span className="rw-sb-label">{label}</span>
38|      {count !== undefined && <span className="rw-sb-count">{count}</span>}
39|    </button>
40|  );

120|// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
121|// ⚡ TDZ GUARD — ALL callback/effect declarations below this
122|// line MUST reference only variables declared ABOVE this line.

125|  const toastTimer = useRef(null);
126|  const showToast = useCallback((msg, action, duration = 2400) => {
127|    if (toastTimer.current) clearTimeout(toastTimer.current);
128|    setToast({ msg, k: Date.now(), action });
129|    toastTimer.current = setTimeout(() => setToast((cur) => (cur && cur.k && Date.now() - cur.k >= duration - 100 ? null : cur)), duration);
130|  }, []);
131|  const promoCloseTimerRef = useRef(null);
132|// ── ALL NEW useCallback/useEffect declarations go below ──
133|  // The survey overlay uses pointer-events: none (clicks pass through).
134|  // Adding a new state AFTER this point will break the site with a TDZ error.
135|  const customProductsRef = useRef(customProducts);

142|  // Load custom products from Supabase & re-check URL hash for direct product links
143|  useEffect(() => {
144|    getCustomProducts().then((prods) => {
145|      if (prods.length) setCustomProducts(prods);
146|      // Re-check the URL hash after custom products load — the hash-change
147|      // handler from the other effect only fires on *changes* to the hash,
148|      // so a direct navigation to #/product/<custom-id> on first page load
149|      // would miss custom products that hadn't loaded from Supabase yet.
150|      if (window.location.hash.startsWith('#/product/')) {
151|        const pid = window.location.hash.replace('#/product/', '');
152|        const allProds = [...REWIND_PRODUCTS, ...prods];
153|        const p = allProds.find(x => (x.id || x.product_id) === pid);
154|        if (p) setSelectedProduct(p);
155|      }
156|    });
157|  }, []);

159|  // Load wishlist from Supabase on mount / email change
160|  useEffect(() => {
161|    if (userEmail) {
162|      getWishlist(userEmail).then((ids) => {
163|        // Merge loaded IDs with any items already in state (e.g. a pending
164|        // wishlist item added by handleSignup during the signup flow, before
165|        // getWishlist resolves). Without merging, the async Supabase response
166|        // overwrites locally-added items and they silently disappear.
167|        setWishlist((prev) => {
168|          if (!ids.length) return prev;
169|          const merged = [...ids];
170|          prev.forEach((id) => {
171|            if (!merged.includes(id)) merged.push(id);
172|          });
173|          return merged;
174|        });
175|        setWishlistReady(true);
176|      });
177|    } else {
178|      // Load from localStorage cache immediately
179|      try {
180|        const cached = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('rw_wishlist') || '[]');
181|        if (cached.length) setWishlist(cached);
182|      } catch {}
183|      setWishlistReady(true);
184|    }
185|  }, [userEmail]);
186|
187|  // Persist wishlist to Supabase — only after initial load
188|  useEffect(() => {
189|    if (!wishlistReady) return;
190|    if (userEmail) {
191|      saveWishlist(userEmail, wishlist);
192|    }

194|  }, [wishlist, userEmail, wishlistReady]);

225|    document.body.style.overflow = anyOpen ? 'hidden' : '';

228|  }, [quick, drawer, checkout, signupOpen, showSizes, infoPage, promoOpen, wishlistOpen, showReferral, showSettings]);
229|
230|  // Mouse-following glow — REMOVED (caused stacking issues with panels/modals)
231|
232|  // Close modals/drawers on Escape key
233|  useEffect(() => {
234|    const onKey = (e) => {
235|      if (e.key !== 'Escape') return;
236|      if (promoOpen && !promoClosing) {
237|        setPromoClosing(true);
238|        promoCloseTimerRef.current = setTimeout(() => { setPromoOpen(false); setPromoClosing(false); promoCloseTimerRef.current = null; }, 300);
239|      }
240|      if (quick !== null)    setQuick(null);
241|      if (drawer)           setDrawer(false);
242|      if (checkout)         setCheckout(false);
243|      if (signupOpen)       setSignupOpen(false);
244|      if (showSizes)        setShowSizes(false);
245|      if (infoPage !== null) setInfoPage(null);
246|      if (wishlistOpen)     setWishlistOpen(false);
247|      if (showReferral)    setShowReferral(false);
248|      if (showSettings)    setShowSettings(false);
249|      // Dismiss survey on Escape only when it's actually visible — prevents
250|      // permanently hiding the first-visit survey for new users who press
251|      // Escape to close a modal/popup/drawer before the survey was dismissed.
252|      // NOTE: showSurvey deliberately omitted from deps to prevent the minifier
253|      // from hoisting this effect before showSurvey's state variable is initialized (TDZ bug).
254|      // showSurveyRef is used instead since refs are stable across hoisting.
255|      if (showSurveyRef.current) {
256|        localStorage.setItem('rw_survey_done', '1');
257|        setShowSurvey(false);
258|      }
259|      if (selectedProduct)  { setSelectedProduct(null); window.history.replaceState({}, '', window.location.pathname); }
260|    };
261|    window.addEventListener('keydown', onKey);
262|    return () => {
263|      window.removeEventListener('keydown', onKey);
264|      if (promoCloseTimerRef.current) { clearTimeout(promoCloseTimerRef.current); promoCloseTimerRef.current = null; }
265|    };
266|  }, [promoOpen, quick, drawer, checkout, signupOpen, showSizes, infoPage, wishlistOpen, showReferral, showSettings, selectedProduct]);
267|
268|  const products = useMemo(() => {
269|    const allProducts = [...REWIND_PRODUCTS, ...customProducts];
270|    return allProducts.filter((p) =>
271|      (cat === 'All' || p.cat === cat) &&
272|      (!brand || p.brand === brand) &&
273|      (query.trim() === '' || (p.name + ' ' + p.cat + ' ' + (p.brand || '') + ' ' + (p.note || '') + ' ' + (p.material || '')).toLowerCase().includes(query.toLowerCase()))
274|    );
275|  }, [cat, brand, query, customProducts]);
276|
277|  // Compute categories that actually have products (including custom products)
278|  // Also appends any categories created via the admin panel's custom-category
279|  // input that aren't already in REWIND_CATS.
280|  const availableCats = useMemo(() => {
281|    const allProds = [...REWIND_PRODUCTS, ...customProducts];
282|    const available = new Set(allProds.map(p => p.cat).filter(Boolean));
283|    const base = REWIND_CATS.filter(c => c === 'All' || available.has(c));
284|    const extras = [...available].filter(c => !REWIND_CATS.includes(c));
285|    return [...base, ...extras];
286|  }, [customProducts]);

288|  const cartCount = cart.reduce((s, it) => s + it.qty, 0);
289|
290|  // Apply dark mode on mount and when it changes
291|  useEffect(() => {
292|    if (darkMode) document.documentElement.classList.add('dark');
293|    else document.documentElement.classList.remove('dark');
294|    localStorage.setItem('rw_theme', darkMode ? 'dark' : 'light');
295|  }, [darkMode]);
296|
297|  // ── ALL new state vars for modals/panels MUST go above this line ──
298|  // succession so the final toast Undo restores ALL of them, not just the last.
299|  const pendingRestoreRef = useRef([]);
300|  const restoreTimerRef = useRef(null);
301|  // Buffered undo for wishlist removals — same pattern as cart undo above.
302|  const pendingWishlistRestoreRef = useRef([]);
303|  const wishlistRestoreTimerRef = useRef(null);
304|  // Buffered undo for recently-viewed "Clear" button — saves the full list so
305|  const recentlyViewedBufferRef = useRef([]);
306|  const recentlyViewedTimerRef = useRef(null);
307|  // Scroll position memory — saves the Y offset before opening a product
308|  // detail page so that clicking "Back" restores the user exactly where they
309|  // were in the grid, rather than snapping them to the top of the page.
310|  const scrollPosRef = useRef(0);
311|  // ── ALREADY DECLARED at top of TDZ guard — do not re-declare ──
312|  // Extract RecentlyViewed handlers to eliminate duplication between product-page and shop views
313|  const handleRecentlyViewedSelect = useCallback((p) => {
314|    const pid = p?.id || p?.product_id;
315|    if (p && pid) {
316|      setSelectedProduct(p);
317|    } else if (pid) {
318|      setRecentlyViewed(prev => prev.filter(x => (x.id || x.product_id) !== pid));
319|      showToast('This product is no longer available');
320|    }
321|  }, [showToast]);
322|
323|  const handleRecentlyViewedClear = useCallback(() => {
324|    setRecentlyViewed((prev) => {
325|      // Buffer the ENTIRE list from state (not the child's filtered `items` arg)
326|      // so Undo can restore every item including the current product when the
327|      // user clicks "Clear" from the product detail page.
328|      recentlyViewedBufferRef.current = [...prev];
329|      return [];
330|    });
331|    if (recentlyViewedTimerRef.current) clearTimeout(recentlyViewedTimerRef.current);
332|    recentlyViewedTimerRef.current = setTimeout(() => { recentlyViewedBufferRef.current = []; }, 2800);
333|    showToast('Recently viewed cleared', {
334|      label: 'Undo',
335|      onClick: () => {
336|        setRecentlyViewed((prev) => {
337|          // Only restore items not already present (e.g. if user
338|          // navigated to a new product during the window)
339|          const saved = recentlyViewedBufferRef.current || [];
340|          const merged = [...prev];
341|          saved.forEach((item) => {
342|            const pid = item.id || item.product_id;
343|            if (pid && !merged.find(x => (x.id || x.product_id) === pid)) {
344|              merged.push(item);
345|            }
346|          });
347|          recentlyViewedBufferRef.current = [];
348|          if (recentlyViewedTimerRef.current) clearTimeout(recentlyViewedTimerRef.current);
349|          return merged;
350|        });
351|      },
352|    });
353|  }, [showToast]);
354|
355|  const handleRecentlyViewedRemove = useCallback((pid, name) => {
356|    // Use ref instead of raw recentlyViewed to prevent stale closure;
357|    // follows the same ref pattern as showSurveyRef, customProductsRef, wishlistRef.
358|    const removedItem = recentlyViewedRef.current.find(p => (p.id || p.product_id) === pid);
359|    if (!removedItem) return;
360|    setRecentlyViewed((prev) => prev.filter(p => (p.id || p.product_id) !== pid));
361|    showToast((name || 'Item') + ' removed', {
362|      label: 'Undo',
363|      onClick: () => {
364|        setRecentlyViewed((prev) => {
365|          // Only restore if not already present
366|          if (prev.find(p => (p.id || p.product_id) === pid)) return prev;
367|          return [removedItem, ...prev];
368|        });
369|      },
370|    });
371|  }, [showToast]);
372|
373|  const addToCart = useCallback((p, size, qty = 1) => {
374|    // Guard: don't allow adding out-of-stock items
375|    if (p.stock === 0) {
376|      showToast(p.name + ' is sold out');
377|      return;
378|    }
379|    const sz = size || p.sizes?.[0] || 'One size';
380|    const pid = p.id || p.product_id;
381|    const key = pid + '-' + sz;
382|    setCart((c) => {
383|      const found = c.find((it) => it.key === key);
384|      if (found) return c.map((it) => it.key === key ? { ...it, qty: it.qty + qty } : it);
385|      return [...c, { key, id: pid, name: p.name, price: p.price, was: p.was, hue: p.hue, img: p.img || '', size: sz, qty: qty }];
386|    });
387|    showToast((qty > 1 ? qty + '× ' : '') + p.name + ' added to bag');
388|  }, [showToast]);
389|
390|  const quickAdd = useCallback((p) => { addToCart(p); setDrawer(true); }, [addToCart]);
391|  const addFromQuick = useCallback((p, size) => { addToCart(p, size); setQuick(null); setDrawer(true); }, [addToCart]);
392|  const changeQty = useCallback((key, d) => { 
393|    setCart((c) => {
394|      const item = c.find(it => it.key === key);
395|      if (!item) return c;
396|      const newQty = item.qty + d;
397|      if (newQty <= 0) {
398|        if (d < 0) {
399|          setPendingRemove({ key, name: item.name });
400|          return c.map(it => it.key === key ? { ...it, qty: 1 } : it);
401|        }
402|        return c;
403|      }
404|      return c.map((it) => it.key === key ? { ...it, qty: newQty } : it); 
405|    }); 
406|  }, []);
407|  const [pendingRemove, setPendingRemove] = useState(null);
408|  const removeItem = useCallback((key, name) => { 
409|    // Capture the removed item so Undo always restores the right data,
410|    // regardless of subsequent cart changes before the user clicks Undo.
411|    const removedItem = cart.find(it => it.key === key);
412|    setCart((c) => c.filter((it) => it.key !== key));
413|    // Accumulate into the pending-restore buffer so rapid removals don't
414|    // silently drop earlier undo actions (showToast replaces the current toast).
415|    if (removedItem) {
416|      pendingRestoreRef.current = [...pendingRestoreRef.current, removedItem];
417|    }
418|    // Clear the buffer when the toast auto-dismisses (slightly after the toast
419|    // duration so there's no race with a user clicking Undo in the final ms).
420|    if (restoreTimerRef.current) clearTimeout(restoreTimerRef.current);
421|    restoreTimerRef.current = setTimeout(() => { pendingRestoreRef.current = []; }, 2600);
422|    const count = pendingRestoreRef.current.length;
423|    const msg = count > 1
424|      ? `${count} items removed`
425|      : (name || 'Item') + ' removed';
426|    showToast(msg, {
427|      label: 'Undo',
428|      onClick: () => {
429|        setCart((c) => {
430|          let next = [...c];
431|          pendingRestoreRef.current.forEach(item => {
432|            if (item && !next.find(i => i.key === item.key)) {
433|              next.push(item);
434|            }
435|          });
436|          pendingRestoreRef.current = [];
437|          if (restoreTimerRef.current) clearTimeout(restoreTimerRef.current);
438|          return next;
439|        });
440|      },
441|    });
442|  }, [cart, showToast]);
443|  const goCheckout = useCallback(() => { setDrawer(false); setCheckout(true); setCheckoutCount(c => c + 1); setPromoOpen(false); setPromoClosing(false); setOrderNumber(''); }, []);
444|  const orderPlaced = useCallback(() => { setCart([]); setCheckout(false); setOrderNumber(''); }, []);
445|
446|  const handleWishlist = useCallback((p) => {
447|    const pid = p.id || p.product_id;
448|    if (!pid) return;
449|    if (!userEmail) {
450|      setPendingWishlistId(pid);
451|      setSignupOpen(true);
452|      return;
453|    }
454|    // Determine whether the item was in the wishlist INSIDE the functional
455|    // setter — React executes updaters synchronously (the variable below is
456|    // set before the code continues), eliminating the stale-closure bug that
457|    // could show the wrong toast when users click the heart rapidly.
458|    let willBeRemoved = false;
459|    setWishlist((prev) => {
460|      const exists = prev.includes(pid);
461|      willBeRemoved = exists;
462|      return exists ? prev.filter((id) => id !== pid) : [...prev, pid];
463|    });
464|    if (willBeRemoved) {
465|      showToast(p.name + ' removed', {
466|        label: 'Undo',
467|        onClick: () => setWishlist((inner) => inner.includes(pid) ? inner : [...inner, pid]),
468|      });
469|    } else {
470|      showToast(p.name + ' saved', {
471|        label: 'Show',
472|        onClick: () => setWishlistOpen(true),
473|      });
474|    }
475|  }, [userEmail, showToast]);
476|
477|  const handleSignup = useCallback(({ email, acceptMarketing }) => {
478|    setUserEmail(email);
479|    setSignupOpen(false);
480|    signupUser(email, acceptMarketing);
481|    if (pendingWishlistId) {
482|      setWishlist((prev) => prev.includes(pendingWishlistId) ? prev : [...prev, pendingWishlistId]);
483|      // Look up product name for a personalised toast
484|      const allProds = [...REWIND_PRODUCTS, ...customProducts];
485|      const pendingProduct = allProds.find(p => (p.id || p.product_id) === pendingWishlistId);
486|      setPendingWishlistId(null);
487|      showToast((pendingProduct?.name || 'Item') + ' saved', {
488|        label: 'Show',
489|        onClick: () => setWishlistOpen(true),
490|      });
491|    }
492|  }, [pendingWishlistId, showToast, customProducts]);
493|
494|  const applyPromo = useCallback(async () => {
495|    if (!promoCode || promoLoading) return;
496|    setPromoLoading(true);
